Major Demonstration by Former American Communists in Chicago Outside Japanese Consulate 82

Protesting Japan's Forced Occupation of the Eastern Provinces

Clash with Steel-Helmeted Police

⊙Chicago: Today, 600 communists surrounded the Japanese Consulate here, protesting Japan's occupation of Manchuria, and clashed for a long time with 200 steel-helmeted police sent by the authorities to suppress them, causing traffic in the city center to be blocked for more than an hour. 184 demonstrators were arrested, including 22 women, such as Remisen, a member of the National Unemployed Committee, and Ms. Nongtai'er, a former teacher at the city's municipal school. When the demonstrators held banners with the words "Get out of China" and crowded into the circular area, the police, knowing the seriousness of the situation, urgently issued a riot alarm. The authorities immediately sent a reserve team and 25 mounted patrols, a total of about 200 people, to suppress them. At that time, the number of demonstrators had increased to 400, and they threw three packs of red pepper powder at the police. However, most of the pepper powder blew back into the eyes of the demonstrators, causing more than 5,000 people to be temporarily blinded. Afterwards, another 200 demonstrators rushed out from the small roads on both sides, and the conflict area expanded. They advanced and retreated around the Chicago Tribune Building Tower. When the fighting between the two sides was fierce, the Japanese Consul Mutō once peered out in front of the office, but the demonstrators were busy resisting the police and did not notice. In the end, the police surrounded the demonstrators and drove them across the canal bridge to Lake Street, where there were fewer vehicles, making it easier for the police to cope, and then dispersed the rioters. Throughout the entire incident, the rioters never attempted to enter the Chicago Tribune. Their sole purpose was clearly to oppose Japan's occupation of Manchuria. It was reported that nearly 100 anti-Japanese banners were seized afterwards. (National Telegram, 28th)

Hitler Appointed German Chancellor, Papen Appointed Vice-Chancellor with Real Power 83

Reuters, Berlin, 29th: According to the opinions of many politicians, President Hindenburg's solution to the political crisis is to make Hitler a puppet chancellor and Papen vice-chancellor, but with real power. The powers of the vice-chancellor will be expanded, and no administrative plan can be established without his approval. President Hindenburg is unwilling to allow Reichstag President Göring to join the cabinet.

Reuters, Berlin, 28th: Schleicher has submitted his resignation to President Hindenburg today, and the president has accepted it and asked former Chancellor Papen to inquire from various political parties and report on whether a new government can be formed based on a broad parliamentary foundation. It is reported that President Hindenburg asked Schleicher to attend the Reichstag and present his policies to await development. Schleicher was unwilling to comply with this request and asked the president to discuss the political situation with his colleagues. The result was that the cabinet decided to resign. The Schleicher cabinet was the twentieth cabinet since the establishment of the German Republic. Schleicher was in office for only 65 days. Many newspapers expressed their opinions, saying that Schleicher previously attacked Papen behind the scenes, forcing President Hindenburg to reluctantly abandon his friend. The president seems to have not forgotten this matter. Also, the fall of the Brüning cabinet was also the responsibility of Schleicher. What Schleicher did to others in the past is now being repaid to him, so he could not keep his position.

Very Difficult for Various Parties to Unite 84

Guomin News Agency, Berlin, 28th: The German political situation is still in extreme chaos today, and there is no hope of clarification or stabilization within the next few days. Since the Schleicher cabinet resigned at 1:00 PM today and the president appointed former Chancellor Papen to investigate the possibility of forming a parliamentary cabinet, the only real development is the decision of the Reichstag Standing Committee to adjourn the Reichstag indefinitely, probably until a new government is formed. However, all parties in the political circles are very skeptical about whether President Hindenburg's imagined parliamentary government, or a cabinet based on the open support of a large majority in the Reichstag, can be realized. Because if the various right-wing parties want to unite, they must first reconcile the old enmities between Hugenberg and Hitler, which is already extremely difficult. And even if the various right-wing parties can unite, they cannot reach a majority in the Reichstag. Therefore, they must also try to win over the Catholic Center Party, which is deeply hated by the National Socialist and German National People's Parties. Therefore, not only is it impossible for the National Socialist and German National People's Parties to accommodate the Center Party, but even the Center Party's hope of supporting Papen's cabinet is absolutely渺茫, because Papen used to belong to the Center Party, but later, due to power relations, he attempted to split the internal part of the party, so he is suspected of betraying the party.

Center Party Plays a Decisive Role 85

Reuters, Berlin, 28th: Supporters of the Republic in Germany are panicked because of the failure of the Schleicher cabinet and the appearance of former Chancellor Papen trying to organize a new cabinet with the powers of a dictator. President Hindenburg instructed Schleicher to present the president's policies to the Reichstag, but Schleicher was unwilling to do so, so he submitted his resignation. Supporters of the Republic believe that Papen's reappointment is a challenging move to the Republic. Hundreds of telegrams have been sent to the president opposing the reinstatement of Papen as chancellor. The most powerful of these comes from the National Trade Union, which asks the president to resolve the political situation in accordance with the constitution and asks the president to meet with representatives of the trade union. Judging from the phenomenon, either Papen or Hitler will be the next chancellor, but the president has instructed Papen to inquire about the opinions of various political parties, in order to know the possibility of the future. Papen has not yet received the order to form a cabinet. The discussions between the National Socialist Party and the German National People's Party have not yet reached a point where both sides can reach a compromise, and the Center Party is standing by. It is allowed that the Center Party has a decisive influence on the organization of the government based on the constitution, so Papen will first devote himself to seeking the assistance of the Center Party.

Berlin Has Several Alarms a Day 86

Guomin News Agency, Berlin, 29th: Yesterday afternoon, former German Chancellor Papen contacted the leaders of various right-wing parties and the leaders of the Center Party and the Bavarian People's Party until late at night. He resumed negotiations this morning, but so far no concrete results have been heard. As for the various political parties and the general public, they are panicked and have several alarms a night. Last night, the Communist Party distributed leaflets instructing workers to prepare for a general strike and convened sales staff from various factories in Berlin to discuss the situation on Monday. The police then ordered the Communist Party to prohibit various outdoor demonstrations planned for today. However, the capital is still calm and there is no serious unrest in the country.

Guomin News Agency, Berlin, 28th: It is heard that outgoing Chancellor Schleicher advised President Hindenburg to solve the political crisis by having Hitler organize a parliamentary government and cautioned the president against any government hanging the false name of the president's office, which in reality only benefits one party. This will be criticized by the majority of the country.

Various Countries React Differently 87

Guomin News Agency, Paris, 29th: Today, French newspapers published the news of the resignation of the German cabinet in a prominent position, mostly believing that it was a sign that the right wing would win in German domestic politics. As for the diplomatic aspect, it seems that there is no need to pay too much attention.

Guomin News Agency, Rome, 29th: The Italian newspapers were very surprised by the resignation of the Schleicher cabinet in Germany, because the Italian people believed that the position of the French cabinet was far more solid than it actually was.

Guomin News Agency, Vienna, 29th: The Austrian capital expressed regret upon hearing the news of the resignation of German Chancellor Schleicher, because the Austrian political circles have always admired and sympathized with Schleicher.

The Future of the French Political Crisis Is Difficult, President-Style Consultation on Prime Ministerial Candidates 88

Reuters, Paris, 28th: French President Lebrun continued to consult with party leaders this morning and afternoon in order to resolve the political crisis. The president also convened financial leaders from both houses of parliament for a meeting, which shows that the president is well aware that the crux of the current political crisis also lies in the financial aspect. It is difficult to predict when the current political crisis will end. There are calls for the left-wing radicals Taladier and Senate Speaker Jeannency to be appointed as prime minister.

Reuters, Paris, 28th: This morning, after the cabinet members left the presidential palace, President Lebrun left Pangue alone in the palace to discuss for a quarter of an hour in order to arrange the approval of the appropriation bill on January 31, because the national treasury is currently empty. It is heard that this move can be done constitutionally, even if the new cabinet is not established by the end of this month, the Senate and the House of Representatives can also accomplish this necessary procedure.

Various Opinions Are Very Divided 89

Havas News Agency, Paris, 28th: How did all parties feel on the first day of the political crisis? There is no indication. All parties unanimously believe that although the Pangue cabinet has been overthrown, the difficulties of the situation have not been reduced. Whoever takes over as prime minister will face difficulties in the House of Representatives, and the situation will be the same as what Pangue experienced. As for the senators, they have fewer concerns about the voters, so they are not as strict with the government as the House of Representatives. Although the split between the Socialist Party and the Radical Socialist Party is not irreparable, the feelings between them are not very harmonious. It will take various tricks to reconcile them. In the House of Representatives' lounge, the general opinion is that Interior Minister Xu Dang and former Army Minister Taladier have some hope of organizing a new cabinet. As for the idea of not organizing a new cabinet exclusively with representatives of the left wing, most believe that it is impossible, unless the Socialist Party refuses to cooperate with the national coalition cabinet or the all-party concentration cabinet, then it is another matter. In the Senate lounge, there were many discussions, and the senators all held a reserved attitude, but some also said that Xu Dang and Daladier had hope of forming a cabinet. Most senators believe that if the government wants to take resolute measures on political affairs, it must be organized by all parties in concentration, but they said that it is not yet time to organize a concentrated cabinet. When Socialist Party leader Blum left the presidential palace, he told people that the Socialist Party still believed that the position of the majority party in the parliament should not change direction, and that the current political crisis would not affect the party's主張.

Taxpayers Resist Tax Increase 90

Havas News Agency, Paris, 28th: The National Union of Taxpayers, with 700,000 members, convened a grand meeting this afternoon to resist tax increases. The meeting place was already overcrowded, and people outside the door were still crowding to enter the meeting place. About a thousand people who were dispersed by the police. After the meeting, some people planned to form a team to demonstrate towards the Senate, the House of Representatives, and the Presidential Palace, but they were eventually dispersed by the police. A conflict occurred between the two sides, and several people were arrested and immediately released. A resolution was unanimously passed at the meeting, requiring ㈠ immediate reduction of the state's useless spending, ㈡ improvement of administration, ㈢ abandonment of the state's overly cumbersome duties, ㈣ reduction of excessive tax rates, and ㈤ creation of bonds to clarify finances in order to restore financial balance, and requesting the President to establish a detached government to govern the country, so as not to be affected by party factions.

Disarmament Conference Affected 91

Havas News Agency, Geneva, 28th: The French political crisis has the danger of making the disarmament conference issues more complicated. The general opinion here is to hope that the French cabinet crisis will be resolved quickly, so that major international issues will not be delayed too much. The Disarmament Conference has organized a committee to study the issue of private manufacturing of armaments within the domestic scope of various countries. This committee was originally scheduled to meet today, chaired by French representative and Vice Minister Gutt. Now, due to the overthrow of the French cabinet, the situation has changed, and it is feared that the UK's proposal on the future working methods of disarmament will be difficult to put forward for discussion. French people at the Disarmament Conference have a very good impression of this proposal, while Germans are very disappointed. The German delegation believes that the British proposal is only intended to seek a mediation method between the Hoover-Simon and French proposals, as well as the Disarmament Conference resolution in December last year. From the point of view of the quality of armaments, Germany firmly demands the principle of equality of armaments and implements it immediately, and the armaments that Germany cannot retain should also be destroyed by other countries. As for the quantity of armaments, Hoover once requested a reduction of two-thirds, while Germany believes that it should implement the "relative" principle according to that country's interpretation of Article 8 of the League of Nations Covenant.

Taladier's Call Is Very High 92

Havas News Agency, Paris, 29th: President Lebrun resumed consultations on cabinet formation at 9:15 this morning, meeting with the leaders of the major party groups in the Senate and the House of Representatives. According to the opinions expressed by the consulted dignitaries, the political situation does not seem to have been clarified. House of Representatives Republican Left Party President Bertier and People's Democratic Party President Simon both said that the Radical Socialist Party cabinet, with Xu Dang who is preparing to concentrate the government as prime minister, is currently impossible. As a result, representatives of various political parties mediating between the Socialist Party and the Radical Socialist Party advocate organizing Taladier as prime minister, and Congress Radical Socialist Party President Taladier as prime minister. The Senate side also proposed Senate Speaker Yenaman, because Yenaman's speech on January 16 made a very good impression.

Havas News Agency, Paris, 29th: Last night, political circles rumored that President Lebrun intended to order Senate Speaker Yenaman to organize a cabinet. According to Yenaman's speech on January 16, he strongly advocated that France should be vigilant on its own in order to avoid the continued extension of the previous situation. However, some people said that Yenaman would rather retain the position of Senate Speaker in order to continue to fulfill his task of adjusting the deliberative body in the Senate. Therefore, President Lebrun seems to be planning to change his request to Congress Radical Socialist Party President Taladier to come forward and form a cabinet. Taladier seems to be planning to propose to the Socialist Party to participate in the cabinet based on a definite political program, but it is very doubtful whether the Socialist Party can accept it. Therefore, Taladier may come forward to organize a cabinet based on a similar political foundation to the previous Herriot cabinet. In this cabinet, the voice of former Minister of Public Works Peng Lai is the highest for the seat of Minister of Finance.

The Collapse of the Chinese Communist Party 95

｜A Personal Account by Zhu Yizhi After Leaving the Communist Party｜

Mr. Zhu Yizhi, who recently left the Communist Party, gave a very detailed account of "The Collapse of the Chinese Communist Party." It is recorded as follows:

1. I was originally a loyal believer in the Communist Party. I have been in the Communist Party for seven years. Now I am standing on the front line against communism.

My political transformation this time came after a day and night of contemplation. This day and night was a chasm in my life. Before this day and night, I was a supporter of communism, a loyal believer in the Communist Party. After this day and night, I became the bravest anti-communist pioneer.

Although a day and night is only twenty-four hours, a very short time, within this short time, I was like two different people. However, this cannot show that I am weak-willed, fickle, or inconsistent, because I have been in the Communist Party for seven years. In these long years, there was not a single moment when I did not fight for communism. I was arrested and imprisoned, subjected to inhuman torture. I fought hand-to-hand with the so-called "enemy" on the battlefield and was seriously wounded more than once. I fled to the mountains and forests, without a grain of rice in my stomach for three days. I used to get up at 5 am every morning and wait outside the factory gate in heavy snow and rain until 1 am at night before I could sleep. I continued this difficult and arduous life for seven years, and I did not change my attitude at all. I did not waver in my belief in the slightest. But this time, I changed my beliefs within twenty-four hours. The reason is very simple: it is my seven years of bloody experience. In the seven years of hard struggle, I deeply understood that communism is not suitable for China's national conditions, and the Communist Party is an obstacle to the Chinese revolution. To complete the Chinese revolution, we must first eliminate and destroy the Chinese Communist Party, which is destroying the Chinese revolution. Therefore, I resolutely and without hesitation moved from the ranks of the Communist Party to the anti-communist front line of the Three Principles of the People.

2. My family was originally wealthy farmers and also owners of handicraft businesses. As a result of imperialist plunder and the shackles of feudal remnants, my family began to go bankrupt when I started school. By the time I entered middle school, my family could not provide any money for my tuition. This historical whip urged me to join the Kuomintang at the age of fourteen. Of course, after joining the Kuomintang, I worked very hard. Therefore, the Communist Party used various methods to win me over. In September of the fifteenth year, I joined the Communist Youth League under the dogmatic propaganda that "the Communist Party is helping the National Revolution, it can strengthen the National Revolution, promote the realization of the Three Principles of the People, and walk from the road of the Three Principles of the People to a communist society." The following year, in February, while studying at the Wuhan Central Military Academy, I joined the Communist Party. At that time, under the slogan of fighting for the "leadership of the Chinese revolution," I worked hard. After the Nanjing purge, under the slogan of "Down with the bourgeoisie who betrayed the revolution," I participated in the Western Expedition (i.e., fighting with Yang Sen and Xia Douyin's troops). When the Wuhan purge took place, the Central Military Academy was disbanded and reorganized into the Fourth Army Training Regiment, which was then transferred to Jiujiang and disarmed. I fled to Zhenjiang, Yangzhou, and Yancheng, lingering for several months. In the seventeenth year, I participated in local branch work and was then transferred to serve as the secretary of the XuhaiBeng Special Committee. In November of the same year, I was arrested and imprisoned until September of the nineteenth year, when I regained my freedom. I served as the director of the Document Section of the Jiangnan Provincial Committee and was then transferred to serve as the secretary of the Railway General Labour Union. Later, I was transferred to be the general secretary of the Jiangsu Provincial General of the Mutual Aid Association. In March of the twentieth year, I served as the director of the Jiangnan District General. In May, I was transferred to serve as the director of the Shanghai Municipal General. In September, I was transferred to be an inspector of the Mutual Aid Association in the outer counties of Jiangsu. In December, I served as a staff member of the General Association's Organization Department. In February of the twenty-first year, I helped with the work of the Hudong District General. In April, I served as the director of the Hudong District General. Soon after, I was dismissed from my work. In August, I was transferred to serve as the secretary-general of the General Association. This is my experience in the Communist Party for seven years, which is also the basis for my firm stance on the anti-communist front line.

3. In these seven years of hard struggle, in these seven years of bloody experience, I deeply felt that:

(1) Since the establishment of the Communist Party, according to the Communist Party's own conclusions, there has not been a single moment when it was not on the wrong path. In the fifteenth and sixteenth years, there was Chen Duxiu's opportunist error. In the sixteenth and seventeenth years, there was Qu Qiubai's blind actionist error. At the Sixth National Congress in the eighteenth year, there were errors regarding the peasant question and the worker movement. Now, the Communist Party has all kinds of disputes, but in the near future, it will surely discover that the lines of the twentieth and twenty-first years are also completely wrong. This raises the question of why the Communist Party is constantly making mistakes. The correct answer to this question is that China is not suitable for the implementation of communism and is not suitable for the existence of the Communist Party. No matter what strategy or line, whether it is left-wing, right-wing, or moderate, it will always be impossible to implement.

(2) According to China's environment and China's economic background, the Chinese revolution should be a national revolution against imperialism, a civil rights revolution to eliminate feudal remnants, and should implement the methods of regulating capital and equalizing land ownership to improve the lives of the people. But the Communist Party's主張, is precisely the opposite, inciting the so-called class struggle to disperse the strength of the national revolution, prolonging the life of feudal forces, and causing all the people, especially workers and peasants, to suffer from bankruptcy, unemployment, and displacement. This is the gift that the Chinese Communist Party has given to the Chinese people.

(3) On the question of anti-imperialism, the Communist Party, under the slogan of "Down with imperialism," is prolonging the rule of商国主义 in China, without any practical anti-imperialist work, and obstructing and destroying the people's anti-imperialist movement. Especially after the January 28th Incident, the Communist Party called for a general strike and peasant uprisings to oppose Japanese imperialism. In fact, this was not opposing Japanese imperialism, but destroying the united front against Japan and disrupting the rear of the resistance against Japan.

(4) Because the Communist Party has completely become an obstacle to the Chinese revolution, its influence among the masses is declining day by day. The masses' response to its calls has changed from passive indifference to active resistance. For example, when it calls for a strike, the workers reply, "This is the Communist Party making trouble," so no strike is initiated by the Communist Party. When it calls for a demonstration, the masses reply, "This is making fun of us," not only do they not participate themselves, but they also advise others not to participate, so no demonstration has any mass participation. When it propagandizes communism to the masses, the masses say, "What is said is good, but it cannot be done," or, "The benefits are in the future, we cannot wait, but at present there are only disadvantages, no advantages." These are all ironclad facts. These ironclad facts shatter the illusions of a very small number of masses about the Communist Party. Therefore, the Communist Party has no mass support at all and is a group of a few bare-handed adventurers.

(5) Since the Communist Party has completely gone bankrupt among the masses, the Communist Party is increasingly moving towards a state of disintegration. Most of the lower-level cadres are dissatisfied with the leadership of the higher-level cadres and continue to put forward dissenting opinions. These lower-level cadres who put forward dissenting opinions are often severely punished and attacked by their superiors and are constantly surrendering to the Kuomintang. In the past few months, more than 500 Communist Party members have surrendered. This astonishing number further proves the collapse of the Communist Party.

(6) Because China's national conditions are not suitable for the existence of the Communist Party, many different opinions have arisen within the Communist Party. These different opinions have become the background for various small organizations in the organization. There is the left-leaning Li Lisan line, and there is the formation of the Li Lisan faction. There is the right-leaning opportunist line, and there is the differentiation of the liquidation faction. There are also the so-called Chen Shaoyu faction, Zhou Enlai faction, and all kinds of other factions. These factions are all trying to save the fate of the Communist Party. However, ironclad facts have proven that this attempt has completely turned into an illusion. No one can stop the collapse of the Communist Party.

(7) The Communist Party is completely in a state of collapse politically and organizationally. The current central faction of the Communist Party, in order to maintain its last rule, on the one hand, uses dogmatic propaganda, saying, "The high tide of the Chinese revolution is coming soon, the initial victory of one or several provinces will be completed soon, and the Chinese Soviet revolution will be successful soon." In this way, it deceives the masses and wins over lower-level cadres. Such propaganda began as early as the eighteenth year, and it has been four years now. The so-called increasingly expanding Soviet area is still a roving bandit that flees east and west. The so-called "revolutionary high tide that is coming soon," the "October Revolution Festival" prepared for three months, resulted in only a few dozen most active cadres. This undoubtedly further disillusions the masses with the Communist Party and causes the cadres of the Communist Party to surrender to the Kuomintang. Therefore, on the other hand, it has no choice but to further adopt the means of red terror and assassination to prolong its last gasp. The recent tragedy in Siven Lane is a concrete manifestation of the Communist Party's assassination policy.

4. In summary, the Communist Party is not suitable for China's national conditions, and no matter what strategy or line it takes, it will be absolutely impossible to implement, it will inevitably not be supported by the masses, and it will inevitably lead to collapse and destruction. The facts have now proven that this assessment is completely correct. But what is the way out for China?

China is a semi-colonial country that is oppressed by the great powers of imperialism on the one hand, and is still bound by feudal remnants on the other, making it impossible for China's politics and economy to get on the right track very quickly. Domestically, there are neither very large landlords nor very large capitalists. Under such circumstances, only the implementation of nationalism can break away from the shackles of imperialism, only the implementation of democracy can complete democratic politics, and only the adoption of the methods of regulating capital and equalizing land ownership can enable the people of society to enjoy their welfare. In other words, only the implementation of the Three Principles of the People can build a new China and enable China to move towards great harmony.

Of course, the current state of China has some aspects that are unsatisfactory. However, there are reasons for this. These reasons are that imperialism has not abandoned its policy of plunder, and feudal remnants still continue to exist, but the main reason is the trouble caused by the Communist Party. Because the Communist Party is actually an assistant to imperialism and feudal remnants. We should not stand in a bystander position to criticize the status quo. We should study the causes of these status quo and make arduous struggles against these causes. In other words, to save China, we must resolutely rise up to eliminate the Communist Party. (Central News Agency)

Ma Hongru Escapes Danger in Yuyu and Arrives in Tianjin 96

＝Arrested by Japanese Army When Yuyu Fell＝

＝Reported to Authorities and Still Went to Front Line＝

Tianjin Correspondence: During the recent Japanese attack on Shanhaiguan County, Ma Hongru, the chief of the Second Branch of the local Public Security Bureau, braved the danger of bullets and arrows to serve as the negotiator. After the city fell, he was arrested by the Japanese army and forced to serve. Ma then responded decisively and designed an escape to Tianjin the other day. He immediately reported the experience to Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong and Civil Affairs Director Wei Jian. The following is a record of Ma's conversation.

The Eve of the Incident 97

Since the establishment of the Boxer Protocol, the Japanese army has occupied the West Main Street in the South Gate of Shanhaiguan, operating foreign firms, pawnshops, and selling drugs. After our country's revolution, they intensified their efforts, establishing gambling houses, resulting in a very complex situation where Chinese, Japanese, and Koreans lived together. Since the September 18th Incident, the local Japanese and Korean people have been unscrupulous and have repeatedly provoked disputes. In August, they forcibly occupied civilian houses and established the "Manchukuo Shanhaiguan Border Monitoring Police Team" (the police force was mostly composed of retired rogue soldiers and gangsters) and the Qin Island Japanese Garrison beat our soldiers. In October, they forcibly occupied the training ground of our 9th Brigade in the East City. On December 8th, Japanese armored vehicles shelled Yuyu City. Provocations were everywhere, in order to create an excuse for aggression. Fortunately, our local authorities and the 9th Brigade Commander He Zhuguo calmly responded, and no major disaster occurred. However, the crisis was still lurking and could erupt at any moment.

The Cause of the Incident 98

On the afternoon of January 1st, at 9 pm, the Japanese garrison stationed in Yuguan sent several soldiers to the Japanese Military Police Detachment Office next to the railway station to throw a grenade. They also threw two grenades in the railway station guardhouse (the Japanese army sentry's rest room) and several grenades near the pseudo-state police team. At the same time, the pseudo-state police team and the Japanese plainclothes team (Japanese residents' military veterans) fired small guns randomly for about an hour and tried to attack the South Gate. Our garrison Commander Shi telegraphed a report to Ping and ordered no retaliation, while sending personnel to negotiate.

The Negotiation 99

At 10 pm that night, I (Chief Ma himself) was ordered to go to the Japanese Military Police Detachment Office to inquire about the situation. At the same time, Chen Ruimin, the chief secretary of the Foreign Affairs Section of our 9th Brigade, also rushed to the scene. They immediately conducted negotiations together. Uno, the chief of the Japanese Military Police Detachment Office, represented the Japanese Garrison Commander Ochiai and warned us that the defense area of the South Gate should be immediately handed over to the Japanese army for guard, with a deadline of 50 minutes for a reply. At 11:05 pm, I and Director Chen entered the city (at this time the city gate had already been closed). At 12:15 am, I went out of the city again to the Japanese Military Police Detachment Office. Unexpectedly, Uno, without waiting for my reply, put forward the following four conditions: (1) Bombs were found at three places, including the Japanese Military Police Detachment Office outside the South Gate tonight, which is very dangerous. For the sake of protecting the railway and the residents, the South Gate will be temporarily guarded by the Japanese garrison. (2) Because the South Gate is guarded by the Japanese army, there are still soldiers from the 9th Brigade's Inspection Office present. To avoid misunderstandings, they must be immediately withdrawn into the city. (3) The police and security team in the South Gate are also afraid of misunderstandings with the Japanese army and must be withdrawn into the city, otherwise, they must gather in the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau and not go out. (4) The sentries of the 9th Brigade on the South City Wall must also be withdrawn to avoid misunderstandings. The entire South Gate will be guarded by the Japanese army. If the above four conditions are not satisfactorily answered, the Japanese army will immediately take free action. I thought that Uno's demands were too unreasonable and immediately reported to the Brigade Headquarters by telephone. Until 4:30 am on the 2nd, our Brigade Headquarters believed that the Japanese demands could not be accepted. The Japanese army was furious, like crazy, and took me to the Japanese Garrison Headquarters.

The Detention Process 100

At 4:35 am on the 2nd, I was escorted by Uno with more than 30 armed soldiers to the Japanese Garrison Headquarters, where I was subjected to insults and unreasonable reprimands. At 10 am, I was sent to the Military Police Detachment Office in the South Gate to monitor me and the 9th Brigade Headquarters communicating by telephone, hoping to trick Staff Officer Yu and Chief of Staff He into the Military Police Detachment Office in order to force them to accept their unreasonable demands. Unexpectedly, the result failed. The Japanese army then implemented climbing the city wall. Our soldiers on the city wall still did not retaliate. When the Japanese soldiers climbed to the top of the city wall, they began to throw stones, causing several to fall and break their legs and arms. Seeing that climbing the city wall had failed, the Japanese army began to shell the city with artillery. At this time, I was sent back to the Japanese Garrison Headquarters for detention.

The Overview of the Battle 101

At 11 am on the 2nd, the Japanese army used mortars to bombard our city from the courtyard of the Military Police Detachment Office. The Japanese Garrison also used heavy artillery to bombard the city. It stopped slightly in the evening. At 8 am on the 3rd, the Japanese navy, army, and air force jointly bombed, mixed with incendiary bombs. At noon, more than a dozen fires broke out in the city, and the smoke billowed into the sky. In the evening, the artillery fire subsided slightly. Our garrison Commander Shi was ordered to abandon the city to prevent the merchants and residents from perishing together. On the morning of the 4th, our army withdrew, and the fires inside and outside the city were raging. The order was greatly disrupted. The Japanese and Korean people and the Japanese army and pseudo-state police carried out large-scale looting and rape. I was forced to serve as the chief of the pseudo-Public Security Bureau to maintain local治安. All actions were under the command of the Japanese Military Police Detachment, and two Japanese soldiers were monitoring me, never leaving me for a moment. On the 6th, gentry and merchants were forced to organize a local maintenance association, and under the orders of the Japanese army, they assisted the pseudo-Public Security Bureau to maintain local治安 and issued notices to persuade merchants and residents to operate as usual. However, the rape and looting by the Japanese and Korean people and the Japanese army did not stop. The Public Security Bureau did not dare to interfere. Shops were forced to open, and goods and money were also robbed. It was not until the 8th, when Brigade Commander Suzuki arrived in Yuguan, that order began to recover slightly, and the fires inside and outside the city gradually extinguished.

The Miserable Situation After the War 102

About 200 shops were burned down, and more than 1,000 houses were damaged. Our army suffered about 500 casualties, and the Japanese army suffered about 400 casualties. About 100 of our residents died, and about 200 were injured. The losses are estimated to be over one million yuan. About 500 or 600 women were raped. Almost all the houses of residents with some assets were looted. The houses of residents that were not destroyed by the artillery fire were occupied by Japanese soldiers. The civilian houses that our army had rented before were regarded as rebel property by the Japanese and were confiscated and will be sold off soon. Our young students and strong men were falsely accused of being reactionary elements, and it is difficult to count those who died unnaturally.

The Japanese Army's Aggression 103

The original plan of the Japanese army was to deceive and open the city gate and carry out the occupation. At the same time, they wanted to take Changli and Luanzhou in one go. Unexpectedly, our army resisted, and morale was indignant. The city exceeded the Japanese army's expectations. Therefore, the Japanese army advanced to the east bank of the Shi River and failed to invade the west. I am a scholar, and fortunately escaped the tiger's mouth. Surviving the danger of bullets and arrows, I have long put my life aside. After reporting to the provincial government this time, I am still willing to go to the front to kill the enemy. (January 27th)

Songjiang 104

Review of Commercial Profits and Losses

Songyi is a rice-producing area. Since the harvest last year, rice prices have plummeted, causing all businesses to decline. Although all industries reduced prices for competitive sales at the end of the year, life was still not prosperous. The following is an exploration of the annual operating profits and losses of various industries: The financial industry, with stable operations, all had surpluses. It is heard that the Xinyu Zhuang surplus was over 10,000 yuan, and Cheng Da's Xingyuan Zhuang and Liang Zhuang each had a surplus of 7,000 yuan. The Kangkang Zhuang is still newly opened and gained a surplus of 4,000 yuan, which is not easy. Pawnshops, banks, and farmers' banks all had surpluses. However, the Songjiang branch of the pawnshop bank has a narrower business scope and not much surplus. The next is the rice industry. Due to the plummeting rice prices in the first half of the year, they suffered heavy losses. The rice prices in various commissions were slightly higher in the second half of the year, but the time was quite short, and the gains did not make up for the losses. Most of them lost money. However, the Beihuitong Rice Shop still had a surplus. The North-South Goods, Medicinal Materials, Bricks, Ash, Oil, and Sesame industries all had surplus profits. The gold shop business was average. However, Defeng closed down and merged into Rifeng. The silk and cloth industry suffered losses due to the influence of Japanese goods. The foreign goods industry was average. The clothing industry suffered losses. The lumber industry only covered expenses. The sock factory was originally a newly emerging industry in Songyi, and the life was quite prosperous. In recent years, due to the war or disaster areas in the sales areas and the tight silver supply, most of them lost money. The cloth factory and carpet industry were slightly better than the sock factory industry, but there were few surplus profits. The new clothing industry also had no surplus due to the heavy eating of capital and poor collection of customer accounts. The Yongmaoheng New Clothing Shop even lost 18,000 yuan and went bankrupt. The Western medicine business was also average. Looking back at the city's business last year, everything was depressed.

Suzhou

Ruling on Appeal in the Labour University Lawsuit 105

In the case where the China General Chamber of Commerce sued the National Labour University Property Custodial Committee for denying a debt of over 200,000 taels, it appealed the first-instance judgment of the Shanghai court to the Jiangsu High Court. Wu Yuxin, the presiding judge of the Civil Second Chamber, tried the case. Yu Shouchun and Luo Yucheng, the agents of the appellant, the General Chamber of Commerce, were present, and lawyers Li Zuyu and Lu Shaozong were retained to present the reasons for the appeal. Tang Ying, the agent of the appellee, the State Labour Committee, also retained lawyers Tan Yigong, Yu Zhong, and Luo to respond. At the end of the trial, the judgment was made on the previous (27th) day. The main text: The original judgment is changed. The principal and interest of the silver owed to the appellant by the former Model Vagrant Two Factories is 100,077,792 taels and 45 cents, and the advance payment is 3,168 taels and 26 cents. Interest shall be given at the normal annual rate of 5% from the date of payment, and the insufficient amount shall be compensated by auctioning off the collateral. The appellee shall be responsible for repaying within the scope of the property left by the former Model Vagrant Two Factories. The remaining appeals and applications for provisional execution are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by both parties.

Wuxi

Deadly Fire Kills Fifteen 106

In Xiyi, outside the North Gate, at No. 36 Heng Street, Chang'an Bridge, the family of Mr. Ding Junxian stayed up all night for the Lunar New Year's Eve. Consequently, they went to sleep on the afternoon of the Lunar New Year's Day (January 26th). Unexpectedly, a stray spark from the morning caused a sudden conflagration, first burning through the staircase. The whole family was sleeping upstairs. By the time they realized it, thick smoke filled the air, and there was no way to escape. Moreover, the wind was strong and the weather was cold. Even when the fire brigades rushed to the rescue, the fire had already spread, making it impossible to extinguish. Ding's wife, Zhao, along with her four sons, one daughter, and the wet nurse, as well as Ding's widowed sister-in-law, Chen, and her one son and three daughters, and the maid Chunlan, totaling thirteen family members, large and small, tragically perished in the blaze. Only Ding Junxian himself and his eleven-year-old son, Xiaoshou, were spared because they went to pay New Year's greetings to relatives and then visited Chong'an Temple. At the same time, a Mr. Chen, formerly a partner in the Renyu sock factory, and his concubine had rented the remaining rooms of the Ding family as their love nest. They were also asleep at the time, and both were tragically caught in the disaster and perished in the fire. Mr. Chen has a wife in Suzhou, who has been notified by relatives via telegram to come to Xiyi to collect the remains.

Export of Rice from Xiyi Reaches 100,000 Shi 107

Since the ban on exporting rice from Jiangsu was lifted, rice merchants have been actively taking advantage of the opportunity. Wuxi, as a rice-gathering area, has seen the export of over 100,000 shi of rice in the past two months. Consequently, the price of rice has risen from seven yuan to around nine yuan, resulting in significant profits. The main exporting firms are Longmao Baoyuan Dafengsheng, Xinchangyuan Hengyi, and others. The rice is transported by train to Beijing and Shanghai, and then transshipped to Tianjin, Bengbu, and Jinan. Most of the purchases are made by rice merchants who come to Wuxi. All expenses, such as transportation fees and passport fees, are borne by the merchants themselves and are not related to the exporting firms. The rice being exported is mostly Qing rice from Zhu Jiage in Qingpu and Wuxi white japonica, followed by white indica.

Changzhou

General Situation of Various Industries After Final Accounting 108

Although the various industries in Wuyi are not as prosperous as those in Suzhou and Wuxi, due to its location in the center of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway and the proximity of Yi, Liyang, and other areas from which people come to Changzhou to make purchases, it used to be above other counties along the line. However, since the January 28th Incident last year, the business of various industries has plummeted, a situation unprecedented. At the time of the business year-end closing, the situation of various industries is briefly recorded as follows: The timber industry is a major industry in Changzhou. Last year, due to the rampant bandits in the production areas, the source of timber was difficult to obtain, and the goods of merchants were burned by the bandits. In addition, foreign pine has taken the place of Western wood, causing great losses to those in this business. The bean industry is also a major industry in Changzhou. Bean prices were low between September and October last year, resulting in no profit. The financial industry was most affected after the Shanghai war. Firms such as Yongli and Runchang closed down one after another. Heshen Company, a decades-old brand, has temporarily suspended the collection of debts. Yongfu, Renfeng, and Tongde are considering forming a bank together. The rest, such as Yifeng, Taicheng, Hongxiang, Yutong, and Zhenkangyuan, are operating as before, but there were no profits at the time of closing. In addition, the decline of the silk and satin and foreign goods industries is also unprecedented. However, oil mills and oil shops have made considerable profits. Xiefeng Oil Mill has a profit of thirty to forty thousand yuan, and Fan Xiesheng Oil Shop also has a profit of twenty to thirty thousand yuan. Next in line is the paper industry, which is also in good condition. The rest are not worth mentioning.

Jiangyin

Economic Decline and Industrial Depression 109

The commerce here was greatly depressed last year due to the influence of the current situation. Since the Fengtai Yuan and Maichang financial firms closed one after the other, there are only two financial firms in Jiangyin, Yongcheng and Xiecheng. Fortunately, the Farmers Bank was established, relying on it to regulate finances. The cloth industry completely stopped trading in the first half of the year. In the second half of the year, it was also greatly impacted by the North China war. Inland river steamers have seen a reduction in passengers due to the through traffic of Chengxi automobiles. However, in order to maintain the livelihood of the staff, they are reluctantly operating, incurring heavy losses. With the exception of small inns that can still be maintained, larger ones such as the Jiangnan Hotel have long been closed. In short, due to the decline of the social economy in the 21st year, the business of various industries has plummeted.

Official Letter

Letter from the Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan 110

To Whom It May Concern: We have recently read a special telegram from Nanjing in your newspaper dated January 27th, which contains a piece of news that Sun Yat-sen, the President of our Yuan, sent a telegram to the authorities in the Southwest, requesting a united resistance against the enemy. After investigation, this does not correspond with the facts. President Sun advocates national unity against the enemy, which is the common desire of the people, but he has not sent this telegram. It is suspected that it is a rumor spread by well-intentioned people, which is being investigated. We hereby request a correction and hope that this letter will be published in your newspaper to clarify the truth.

Sincerely,

The Secretariat of the Legislative Yuan

Local News

Declaration of Solicitation of Members by the Chinese Aviation Association 113

The Chinese Aviation Association was officially established on New Year's Day. Its responsibility is to gather the strength of the people of the country, assist the government, develop aviation, and strengthen national defense. A telegram has already been sent to the compatriots of the country. Now, at the beginning of the Association's solicitation of members, the reasons for the establishment of the Association and the policies to be carried out are declared as follows:

I. The Reasons for the Establishment of the Association 114

Among today's national defense tools, although the sea, land, and air forces are equally important, the air force is the center of gravity. Airplanes can soar through the sky and go wherever they want. Anything from the solidity of strong fortresses, the danger of deep mountains and valleys, and even the vastness of the army and the strength of the navy, from the perspective of the air force, all are unmanned territory. Bombing and sweeping can be done at will. In the past, wars were decided on the battlefield. Today's wars are to subdue the entire country. Once the war breaks out, the air force will be used in a violent manner. All of the enemy's prosperous cities and production centers must be destroyed quickly, either to cut off supplies to the front or to shock the people of the country. We can see from the European War in the distance and the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai in the near future. The need for national defense is therefore the most important for the air force. In addition, the construction of the sea and land forces is more complicated than aviation. The former requires tens of millions, while the latter can be achieved with only a fraction of that. Therefore, for the sake of economy and time, air defense is the easiest. This is why the Association is particularly dedicated to this. Today's war aims to subdue the entire opponent. So, it is of no use to try with all efforts. As the scale of the war increases, the content becomes more complex, and the cost must be greater. Therefore, the government and the people must work together to deal with the enemy. This is inevitable and undeniable. Since the European War, in addition to strengthening military preparations, the responsibility of national defense has gradually shifted from the realm of the military to the entirety of the nation. Military skills are to be taught to everyone. For example, patriotic people and national defense organizations are raising funds to purchase weapons and help the military. The Soviet Russian National Defense Aviation Chemical Association has purchased more than 500 aircraft for the military and raised funds to build aircraft carriers, reaching 15 million rubles in one year. The national defense of the great powers is already strong, but they are still expanding, hoping that the people will work together to overcome difficulties, and the people are also responding vigorously, considering it their duty, and even donating automatically. On the contrary, our country is very different. The territory of the Northeast has been seized, the borders have been removed, and there is no defense. The great powers are sharpening their swords and are ready to explode. The need for national defense is more urgent than in any other country, and the strength of national defense is more limited than in any other country. We are in this situation and witness this situation, how can we not be heartbroken? We know that patriotism and concern for the times are the same for everyone, but we have no way to contribute, so we are hiding and not expressing. There must be a fixed group to vigorously advocate, so that the people of the country and overseas compatriots can base their patriotic heart and release the real strength of saving the country, so that we can get the effect of all people helping together, and use the power of the people to build a city. This is why the Association should meet the needs of the times, and hope to unite the group's strength to help the national defense. In recent years, the strong neighbor has shown fierce flames, and the three northeastern provinces have been looted. The central plains have been ravaged even more. At present, the national situation is difficult, and future worries are even greater. If we procrastinate and let it evolve, the disaster of national subjugation will be inevitable, and we will suffer forever and never recover. In today's world, science is booming, and all advances are being made. Those who destroy the country use their political, economic, and cultural power, all accompanied by military force. They not only impose strict control but also refine the method of exploitation. The people of the victorious countries have no way to resist, and they are becoming increasingly poor. They are also imprisoned and taught, using a hundred different ways to make them stupid and docile, and to gradually forget their thoughts about their home country. This makes our country in today's real danger unprecedented. It is not only a matter of temporary safety, but also a matter of the rise and fall of the ages. If we now cheer up, things can still be done. If we do not seek this, it will be too late. This is why the Association wants to alert the eternal extinction of the national vein, and hope to correct fellow people, and to be effective in time.

II. The Implementation Policies of the Association 115

The Association is committed to the fact that aviation has no foundation, and we dare not neglect any expedient measures. The most important thing is to strive for self-reliance, and to plan for long-term development. Although there are many leads, and it is impossible to implement them all immediately, the following matters should be actively planned and completed as soon as possible. (1) Establish an aviation factory. All the aircraft that our country used to have were purchased from foreign countries. There has never been any attempt to build them ourselves. The price is high, and the goods are not of high quality. If we rely solely on purchasing aircraft in the future, the cost will be too high. Once a war breaks out, the source will be cut off. Old machines will break down day by day, and no new machines will be added. We will sit and be bombed by the enemy and have nothing to do. We should set up a factory to manufacture ourselves, so that scholars who have returned home after studying can have a place to make their own efforts, and those who are interested in research can learn. Therefore, the establishment of a factory should be urgently planned to lay the foundation for self-reliance. (2) Establish a civil aviation school. To date, our country only has a military aviation school. The personnel trained there are not enough. To talk about the expansion of aviation with so few people, even if it is done for a hundred years, it will not be remarkable. Therefore, we must train more experts to meet future needs. As for borrowing materials from other places, it is only suitable for the beginning, as a short-term hire. If we do not seek self-reliance and always rely on foreign guests, it will not only cost too much, but also be difficult to use as desired. Moreover, in the event of war, international relations will be strained, and foreign guests may be difficult to help. Therefore, planning the establishment of an aviation school, so as to create a flourishing of talents, is also a plan that cannot be delayed. (3) Develop civil aviation. Aviation has become a means of transportation to make up for the shortcomings of trains and ships. The assistance to air defense should be implicitly implied in it. Pure military equipment is all a waste of money, and it is useless in peacetime. The people are afraid that there is no continuing interest. Therefore, if we want to get the power of civil aviation in wartime, we must make it a daily need in peacetime, and the benefit of the country is in the benefit of the people. This means that civil use is the help of military use. All countries in the world assist private aviation with huge sums of money. Our country has a vast territory and a mild climate. Long-distance flights are most suitable. However, due to the obstruction of traffic and the difficulty of travel, the need for aviation is most urgent. The development of civil aviation is not only the foundation of military preparation, but also the need of the times. All of these require a lot of money, and for the sake of urgently needed aircraft, we have to purchase some. This requires the enthusiastic participation of the people of the country and the joint burden of the Association. It also requires the efforts of people from all walks of life. We also plan to request the government to provide subsidies as appropriate. For the custody and use of these funds, the Association has formulated an aviation fund custody committee to take responsibility for it. We have also settled on regulations to be observed, so as to prevent the abuse of encroachment, and to ensure that there is no waste. All income and expenditure must be open, which is natural and needless to say.

Unifying the Strength of Civil Aviation 116

The Association has something that cannot be said. Since we want to use the power of the people to help the government's air defense, all planning must be convenient for civil use and suitable for the needs of the government's military use. The structure of aircraft, the training of personnel, and all equipment must be uniform, so as to produce the corresponding efficiency. To achieve this, the unification of the strength of civil aviation must first be achieved. Otherwise, it will be complicated and chaotic, each doing its own thing. Even if civil aviation is developed in peacetime, it will not be enough to meet the needs of wartime. Therefore, at the beginning of the establishment of the Association, the unification of the strength of civil aviation was used as a call. This is what the situation demands, and it is not to be done.

Being in the Same Boat, Working Together 117

To sum up, our country not only has the danger of extinction, but the pain of national subjugation is not comparable to the past. We will always suffer for generations to come, and there will be no chance of recovery. Self-help and saving the country are today. Protecting the country requires the joint efforts of the people, which has become the common trend in the world today. The people of our country are rising up spontaneously, and they need to be more urgent than the people of other countries. The way to work is aviation, which is the easiest and most important. The Association is based on the common desire of the people of the country, hoping to make a concrete expression. I believe that we can all cherish the meaning of "when the skin is gone, what will the hair be attached to," and also swear to the sincerity of "everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." With the determination to be in the same boat, working together, the Association assumes the responsibility of advocacy. It is necessary to encourage the heart of chastity, and to make sure that the collection of one piece will become a fur coat, and that one money will be used for one money. Alas, things are urgent, the enemies are deep, and the gentlemen of our country, let's get up and come!

Suggestion to Purchase Public Debt Airplanes 118

The National Salvation Ten-Person Group sent a letter to the holders of domestic public debt, saying, "The national crisis is urgent. The blood of the Battle of Shanghai is still vivid, the beacon smoke in the Northeast has not extinguished. Aviation to save the country is an urgent and temporary solution. However, patriotic organizations are often more than willing but lack the power. Your association represents the highest asset class in the country. Please donate two or three months of principal and interest to purchase a fleet of public debt aircraft to meet the national crisis. After that, donate one month of principal and interest every year as a fund for planning and setting up aviation manufacturing. This matter is of public interest, and the loss to you is very small, but the remedy for the national crisis is great. Please immediately decide to implement it, and directly allocate the funds from the surplus under customs, and work with the government and national salvation organizations to organize a supervisory committee to supervise the use. I think you have a great heart, and you will not deny it and leave it in the middle without issuing it."

Telegram Passed on the Anniversary of the January 28th Incident 119

Four Telegrams Sent Yesterday

When the various sectors of the city held the anniversary of the January 28th Incident at the Youth Propaganda Troupe the day before yesterday (January 28th), four telegrams were passed. The texts were found and recorded below:

(1) Telegram Requesting the People of the Country to Unite Against Japan. Since the January 28th Incident occurred, it has been a year. The lost land of the three provinces has not been recovered, the traces of blood in Shanghai are still vivid, and the news of the police in North China has occurred again. Yuguan has been lost, Rehe is in danger, the volunteer army has collapsed, the thieves are arrogant, the door is open, and the threat of death is imminent. The Japanese warlords are inching forward, and the ambition to destroy our country and nation is obvious. The League of Nations is not reliable, and the enemy's cavalry is driving straight in. If the people of our country do not rise up quickly to resist the enemy and save the sinking, we will see that the ancient country of China will become the continuation of Korea and India. Although the enemy's armaments are superior and inferior, the number of victories and defeats is not entirely dependent on materials. The spirit of the soldiers is also very important. Looking at the Battle of January 28th, our 19th Route Army and the 5th Army fought bloodily with the enemy for 34 days. They persevered and repeatedly thwarted the enemy's ferocity. Although the enemy changed commanders four times and increased reinforcements, they were never able to cross the Leichi step. It can be seen that the national soldiers are loyal and brave to defend the country, and if they are given the benefit of weapons, there is no fear that they will not be able to recover the lost land and drive the strong enemies out of the country. Now, fortunately, the disaster areas along the Yangtze River have gradually recovered, and the bandits in the provinces have been successively suppressed. This is the time when the whole country should concentrate its strength to save the country. I wish that the loyal and brave generals of our country would purge the dangers of death and eliminate the disputes of barbarians, following in the footsteps of the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army, holding a spear forward and fighting to kill the enemy, so as to fulfill the military's duty to defend the country. The compatriots of the country should quickly rise up to be the backing of the government, generously donate, gather huge funds, and help the government purchase aircraft and weapons, so as to increase the strength of resisting the enemy, and strive to boycott goods and strictly sanction traitors, so as to control the economic life of the Japanese. With common planning and common strength, things can still be done. Alas, things are urgent, the situation is pressing. If we do not eliminate the strong enemy, we will not be able to save the country. If we do not recover the lost land, we will not be able to survive. The whole country should make the greatest determination, unite the strength of the whole country, and swear to resist the enemy to death, recover our land, and avoid the danger of the country and the nation. The representatives of Shanghai held a memorial meeting on the first anniversary of the January 28th Shanghai Anti-Japanese War.

(2) Telegram Requesting the League of Nations to Resolve the Northeast Incident and Stop the Aggression of Violent Japan. To the International League of Nations: Since Japan invaded the Northeast, your spirit of maintaining peace is admirable. However, the violent Japan has no ambition, and it has achieved an inch. It has created a false organization with one hand, and has included the three northeastern provinces without remainder. Recently, it has expanded the incident, invaded Yuguan, and invaded the Rehe River. Your association has not taken any concrete measures, which is regrettable. Now that Japan's militarism has forced us to retreat, we have no choice but to continue the spirit of the January 28th Shanghai War and fight to the death with the enemy for the sake of self-help and self-defense of the Chinese nation. At this critical moment, I hope that your association will follow the spirit of the covenant, take resolute and effective measures as soon as possible, and stop the aggressive behavior of the violent Japan. Otherwise, your association should be fully responsible for the rupture of peace in East Asia. The association feels the intensity of the disaster suffered in Shanghai last year and can't bear to see the compatriots in North China suffer the same fate. Therefore, on the occasion of this painful anniversary of January 28th, I would like to make a final sincere appeal to your association on behalf of all sectors of Shanghai.

(3) Telegram Requesting All Generals of the Country to Mobilize to Resist Japan. In the Battle of January 28th, the Japanese warlords claimed that they could occupy Shanghai in four hours. When the war broke out, our 19th Route Army and the 5th Army fought with the enemy for 34 days, so that the enemy changed its commanders four times but could not cross the Leichi step. This spirit of bravely resisting the enemy is enough to express the great power of our nation that cannot be humiliated. It can also be seen that the strength of resisting the enemy is not only in whether there are elite weapons, but also in whether our people have the spirit of independence and self-reliance. The 19th Route Army and the 5th Army have this spirit, so they can chill the enemy and inflict heavy damage on it. If all our soldiers have this spirit, why worry about not being able to recover the lost land and drive the enemy out of the country? Today is the anniversary of the January 28th Incident, and the Japanese warlords who have not been successful in the southeast are thinking of showing their ferocity in our North China. The danger of Yuguan has been lost, and the danger of Rehe is even more urgent. If Rehe is lost, Pingjin will not be guaranteed. If Pingjin is not guaranteed, the country will be destroyed in no time. The soldiers of the whole country should fulfill their duty to defend the country and make a great move to save the country. If they can unify their minds and concentrate their strength, the lost land can be recovered, and the great revenge can be avenged. At the time when foreign insults are serious, it is time for the soldiers of the whole country to serve the country. I hope that we can mobilize together and go to the national crisis together. Then, Shao Kang will prosper Xia with one army, and Xiang Yu will perish Qin with eight thousand. The achievements are the same in ancient and modern times. The survival and continuation are in this one move. The head of the hero is the culprit, and I hope you will choose yourself.

(4) Telegram Requesting the People of the Country to Donate Funds to Purchase Aircraft to Defend the Country. Since the fall of the Northeast and the bloody Battle of Shanghai, the Japanese imperialist's ambition to invade our country has been fully exposed. The people of the country also deeply know that if we do not resist the enemy, we will not be able to talk about saving the country. The way to resist the enemy must be that the soldiers are strong and the weapons are sharp, and then the national defense can be strong. In today's scientific era, aircraft are the only important military equipment for national defense. Since the European War, the great powers have paid attention to it, so the annual expansion is recent. The Japanese industry and commerce have donated funds to purchase aircraft to give to the government for the purpose of enriching the national defense. Looking back at our country, the sea and land military preparations have been behind, and the air force equipment is even more lacking. Therefore, in the Battle of Shanghai and the Battle of Yuguan, our army's combat power was not as good as others, but the enemy was able to drive straight in. From this, we can know that it is difficult to win by relying solely on the sacrifice of flesh and blood. At this time when the international situation is becoming increasingly serious and the situation in North China is becoming increasingly tense, if we do not build an air force and enrich national defense, the country will be destroyed in no time. In addition to supervising the city's residents to donate funds to purchase aircraft, the General Assembly hopes that the people of the country will work together to actively donate funds, and strive to achieve the goal of donating one aircraft per county. It will be a great blessing for the country.

After Today's Final Accounts 131

Business Resumes as Usual from Today

Money Exchanges Also Resume Operations

After the final accounts were settled, various industries in this city traditionally closed for business. Yesterday was the fourth day. According to custom, the God of Wealth is welcomed, so many people were selling carp along the streets. Because carp are commonly known as "yuanbao fish," they are an essential item for welcoming the God of Wealth. After welcoming the God of Wealth, all industries will open for business as usual from today. Money exchanges were originally scheduled to close for four days and will also resume operations as usual from today. However, due to the impact of the January 28th Incident, various industries are extremely depressed. After the final accounts were settled, there were fewer businesses that added capital to continue operating. However, the number of businesses that were unable to maintain operations and ceased operating was numerous.

Liu Zhongying and Others Propose Restoring the Citizens' Volunteer Army 133

Intensify Training and Prepare to Go North to Kill the Enemy

Liu Zhongying, Zhou Zhaolin, Huang Fei and other executive committee members of the Shanghai Special District Citizens' Union, considering the arrogance of the enemy and the daily increasing danger to the nation, believe that only the strength of the entire citizenry is not enough to save the country, and yesterday specially submitted a letter to the Citizens' Union, requesting that the Citizens' Volunteer Army be convened immediately, that training be intensified, and that they go north to kill the enemy. The original letter is recorded below: (Omitted above) Our Citizens' Union, at the time of the September 18th Incident, felt the pain of the invading Japanese devils and the fear of the imminent demise of the country. Thereupon, the Citizens' Volunteer Army was established. The committee members planned with all their hearts and trained through the night, preparing to go to the Northeast and compete with the enemy. This was the duty of the citizenry and also a rare act of distinction for your union. Who knew that the enemy would be aggressive and exhaustive, and, having gained Long, look to Shu, invading the Northeast and then attacking Shanghai. The bloodstains of September 18th were not yet dry, and the tragedy of January 28th was born. Our Citizens' Volunteer Army, volunteered to defend against the enemy, pressing forward despite all obstacles. The enemy's courage was chilled by the battle of Baoshan. Such a tragic and fierce battle cannot but be admired by the people of the nation, and foreigners also praised it. After the Shanghai battle stopped and the peace treaty was signed, the loyal and brave Citizens' Volunteer Army, which defended the country, was unknowingly dissolved. Could it be that the lost territory has been recovered and military preparedness is no longer necessary, or that the Northeast is too far away and assistance is no longer needed? What could be more painful than this? Zhongying and others look to the Northeast and see Peiping and Tianjin. The shouts of the Volunteer Armies and the warnings of the National Army are still loud. Thus, it is known that the hearts of the people are not yet dead and that national affairs can still be done. Therefore, we specially suggest to your union that you convene the Citizens' Volunteer Army again immediately, intensify training, go to the Northeast, and participate in defending against the enemy, so that this shattered China can be made whole again and this declining Chinese nation can be revitalized. Please implement this immediately. We eagerly await your response. This is addressed to the Citizens' Union.
