Spring and Autumn

The Sorrow of a Prodigal Son 206

– Zhan Lu

Zheng Guoyou, the mastermind behind the assassination of Feng Deqian, was tried more than ten times in Hong Kong. Although he hired many foreign lawyers who eloquently defended him in court, he could not escape the special provision of "a murderer must die" and was eventually sentenced to death. A rich man's son with huge sums of money could not prolong his life after all, which is the sorrow of a prodigal son! Zheng Guoyou was the grandson of the late Nanyang Kapitan Zheng Gui. Zheng Gui resided in Perak, Malaysia, and, under the guidance of foreigners, made great contributions to the construction of the opening and closing of Perak, thus becoming a great wealthy man. After becoming rich, he was able to work hard on public welfare affairs and had a good reputation among the overseas Chinese. After Zheng Gui died, his son Jing Tang, that is, Zheng Guoyou's father, also passed away one after another. At this time, Zheng Guoyou was only six years old and became an orphan without ancestors or father. This situation was described by 240 Hong Kong gentlemen and merchants, including Huang Guangtian, in a joint petition, begging the Hong Kong Governor to spare his death. However, the Legislative Council refused the joint petition of the gentlemen and merchants, and could not exempt the death penalty of the unfilial grandson because of the merits of his grandfather. This is the sorrow of a prodigal son!

Zheng's mother went to visit him in prison two weeks ago. Zheng Guoyou had completely changed his former arrogant state, suppressed his grief, and comforted his mother kindly, saying, "In prison, your son has a mattress to sleep on and fish to eat. I hope mother can rest assured." Zheng's mother said with tears in her eyes, "My son is accustomed to being pampered. Now, it is not like being at home. Even if there is no white rice, you have to swallow even burnt rice." Guoyou bowed his head and accepted his fate, tears streaming down his face, which is the sorrow of a prodigal son.

The Hong Kong merchants' joint petition was written by Lai Biao Xi, a former Hanlin scholar of the Qing Dynasty, which contained a passage saying, "Zheng Guoyou was only six years old when he had no strict father to guide him, and he inherited a huge family fortune. His mother was a widow and had no time to teach him about his character or control his actions. As he grew older, his desires gradually opened up. Relying on his wealth, he violated the norms, indulged in irregular entertainment, and made friends with improper and promiscuous friends." He thoroughly described the situation of Guoyou's lack of education, which is the sorrow of a prodigal son!

According to recent news from Hong Kong, the Legislative Council finally complied with the request of the gentlemen and merchants and changed Zheng Guoyou's sentence to life imprisonment. Perhaps, Hanlin Lai's writing had some effect. The petition stated, "A weak young man, ignorant and unknowing, possessed wealth and was coveted by villains who set traps to lure and confuse him, leading to his imprisonment. He is truly pitiful," and so on, achieving a considerable effect. However, what is the difference between life imprisonment and death? Moreover, there is endless suffering, which is the sorrow of a prodigal son!

Wielding Spears and Gentle Sighs 207

— Yan Qiao

｜Retracing the Resistance Against Japanese Pirates｜

After the snow cleared, I thought of the winds and clouds over Yuguan Pass. Coincidentally, a letter arrived from Tan Yaosheng in Chaoyang, saying that Japanese planes had not come for three months. Now, due to the urgent invasion, they are circling again, the situation resembling Suzhou on this day last year. When can we wield the spear of Lu Yang? The more I think about it, the more troubled I become! I happened to read "Random Talks from the Mountains and Seas," recalling the Ming Jiajing era's resistance against Japanese pirates. Devouring a large piece of meat at the butcher's door, I felt a brief moment of satisfaction. "Random Talks" was written by Ren Huan of Changzhou, Ming Dynasty. He rose through the ranks from Jinshi to Deputy Prefect of Suzhou, fighting the Japanese pirates in over one hundred and ten battles, beheading over fifty thousand enemies, and protecting more than twenty cities. One year, Japanese pirates attacked Suzhou, and the city gates were closed during the day, with the people wailing around the city. Ren Huan admitted them during the day, saving tens of thousands of lives. When Japanese pirates seized civilian boats to escape to sea, Ren Huan intercepted them at Maji Mountain, burning those entrenched in Jiading to death. Later generations only know of Qi Jiguang's merit in resisting Japanese pirates, unaware that Ren Huan was the mainstay, like Fang Zhaoyuan to the 19th Route Army. Yet, Ren Huan was but a scholar, truly remarkable. In "Random Talks," there is a "Reduced Character Magnolia Flower" poem about Wusong: "Tossing and turning, when will the incessant autumn rain cease? Warships on the river, charging through the waves for half a year. The ominous atmosphere has not been swept away, and sorrow makes me feel my age. Holding a sword in the west wind, singing慷慨悲歌in wine." Its mournful courage is no less than Yue Wu Mu's "Man Jiang Hong." Other lines include: "The pirate's lair is clearly exterminated, and peace is once again seen in the southeast." "Cultivating oneself is the duty of a man; do not let this turban be worn in vain." "Ten thousand men learning to fight the enemy is futile; only mental strength can defeat the enemy." "With a three-foot sword and ten thousand scrolls, where can a man not make his home?" Reading it fills one with vigor. During his time, poets wrote in praise of him, such as Gui Youguang's "Ren Gong has personally killed the enemy." "Even children know Deputy Administrator Ren, standing tall as a golden city on the sea." Wen Zhengming's "Barbarians from the east suddenly shocked us, but the magistrate's benevolence and martial prowess form a great wall." Tang Shunzhi's "The enemy fears him like Fan and Han, and overseas they call him Lord Ren." Wen Yuan's "Sails brushing Fusang frighten the barbarian lands, and his awe-inspiring presence makes him a heroic general." Wang Guxiang's "How many scholar-generals have been praised throughout history? He truly has armor and weapons in his mind." All highly praised him. Today, reaching Mudu and Pingwang, seeing the perilous watchtowers, one can still imagine the heroic and bloody battles of the martyrs. Four hundred years later, Shanghai and Songhu are once again ravaged, how would Ren Gong feel if he knew? I believe that such texts full of courage and spirit should be made for young students to write ten thousand times and recite a thousand times.

Urban Notebook 208

— Guo Lanxin

｜A Corner of the Human Flesh Market｜

The city is a paradise built upon sin. The appearance of the city is prosperity, the blood of the city is money, and the inner core of the city is carnal desire. Shanghai is such a paradise built upon sin.

Last night, I stepped onto North Sichuan Road, which had been trampled by the Japanese iron hooves. The once luxurious and mysterious street gradually revived after the calamity. When passing the Sichuan Road Bridge, looking north, one can see the streetlights shimmering like a fire dragon. On the smooth asphalt road,

Fiction

Hometown 209

— Hu Tiwei

So, after the prescription was finalized, he immediately sent the long-term worker to a place hundreds of miles away to collect the medicine. Meanwhile, Hongye's brother hurried to a friend's place five miles away to borrow opium paraphernalia because Dr. X liked to smoke a couple of pipes. Father also seemed a little happier, specifically instructing them to order a lavish meal and invite old man Zhang from next door to keep Dr. X company and wash away the dust.

The next day, the doctor left, and the medicine was collected. Just a pair of geckos cost twenty-two dollars. Hongye and her brother personally unpacked the medicine and brewed it carefully, watching the charcoal fire vigilantly. It seemed as if their father's life depended on that small pair of geckos.

After taking three doses, it seemed that the swelling had subsided a little, and Dr. X came again.

"How is it? I said I was confident in treating your father's illness. But fortunately, we caught it early, otherwise, even I would have been helpless. Based on the current situation, after taking about ten doses, the swelling should completely subside."

He wrote five more prescriptions and then stopped. One prescription included velvet antler slices, which had to be obtained from H City.

"This velvet antler is very expensive. It's best if you buy a whole one and slice it yourselves, it will be more cost-effective. Take two hundred dollars with you, that should be enough."

Hongye's brother knew that velvet antler was the most potent thing and wondered if it was suitable to eat. After consulting their father, the result was, "Don't doubt the person you employ, and don't doubt what they prescribe." Following his instructions, they prepared and ate it. Surprisingly, it didn't seem to worsen things, but it didn't get better either.

Dr. X's third act took a complete turn on the opium couch and became increasingly reckless.

"Your father has trouble sleeping at night, it's because his heart and kidneys are not in harmony. Playing with a couple of puffs of this stuff is the most effective treatment, isn't it?"

After a secret meeting between the Hong siblings and their mother, they unanimously agreed that this panacea, not found in any herbal, was feasible. However, knowing that this was something their father deeply hated in his life, they weren't sure if he would break his principles and could only tentatively mention it. As expected, their mother was immediately rebuffed, and their father even scolded the flamboyant Dr. X behind his back. The Hong siblings were so frightened that they dared not speak again.

But at the same time, many people who came to visit their father asked in unison, "Have you tried smoking opium yet?" (5)

Flowing with vehicles, bustling with people.

What I am now exposing is a corner of carnal desire in the city. Such expressions are common in the city. From this, it can be seen that under the oppressed joy lies the misery of many Chinese women who have been corrupted by the social environment, being insulted and trampled upon by foreign beasts in their brutality.

In a coffee shop, right in the middle of North Sichuan Road's showcase from Bazilu to Qiujiang Road, there is an advertisement for red lanterns outside. Inside this coffee shop, besides a few waitresses wearing white vests, there are seven or eight women dressed in colorful clothes. Although their figures are not quite as slender and graceful as urban women, they are all very young. Their faces are covered in powder like plastered walls, and their lipstick is like basins of blood. Some have southern accents, some have northern accents. A woman in her forties leads them. This group specializes in serving foreign guests and soldiers. They seem like a moving machine. When they receive customers, they go with them to secret locations rented by the coffee shop owner on Bazilu to engage in the performance in the fiery pit. The price they receive is about ten dollars, which is split between the coffee shop owner and the procuress-like woman in a ratio of four to six. Several of them already have the smell of sulfur. They are constantly being insulted and trampled upon by foreigners, day after day. Some entertain more than one man each night, and some drunken sailors gang-rape one woman. Ah, it's all for being sold to earn money for the procuress and the coffee shop owner. This place is filled with bloodshed and devoid of light, completely dark, cruel, and reminiscent of a human flesh market-like hell.

Ah, this corner of sin formed in the urban background, I hope the torch of justice and humanity will illuminate it, so that it doesn't remain in darkness forever, and so that these suffering women don't always sink into depravity!

This is what I hope for! This is why I wrote it down.

Radio Drama 210

— Tao

｜A New Perspective｜

Stage plays have sound and color, while silver screen plays have color but no sound (except for "talkies"). Radio dramas, on the other hand, have sound but no color, specifically for entertainment on the radio. The writing of the script differs greatly among the three. Stage plays can accommodate everything: scenery, music, expressions, dialogue, singing, and martial arts. Silver screen plays are slightly different. The script does not necessarily require dialogue from the characters. The plot and emotional appeal can be understood simply by watching the image. Therefore, those who oppose talkies often criticize them as unnecessary. Radio drama scripts are often short plays, suitable for about half an hour. The cast is three or four people, or five or six people. In addition to dialogue, the sounds of animals and objects are all included. In foreign countries, there are many such dramas on the radio. Although radio in China was once very popular, such dramas are still lacking. Recently, Xu Zhuodai has compiled and performed a play for four factories, including the Family Industrial Cooperative, at the Yongsheng Company radio station on December 26, which is truly a groundbreaking initiative. In the future, imitators will surely follow. The actors this time include painter Tao Zhongcheng and five or six others, while the original author of the play is Wang Zhongxian. At the same time, there is also a speech by Yan Duhe, complementing each other. The 28th is the anniversary of the January 28 Incident, so Xu Zhuodai will give a speech about the situation of fleeing Jiangwan at that time, which is said to be extremely poignant.

Local Customs

Suzhou at the Start and End of the Old Lunar Year 211

— Zhu

Although the Gregorian calendar has been used for quite some time, due to the continued customs of the people, the authority of the lunar calendar still holds the upper hand. Over the past twenty-two years, it has turned into a situation where yin prevails over yang. Taking Suzhou as an example, the Gregorian New Year only sees schools and government offices taking a few days off, just a formality. In society, it is still like dealing with the Northeast issue, always in a state of calm. But when it comes to the Lunar New Year, there is a big change. The following notes are about the scenes of Suzhou at the beginning and end of the old lunar year.

㈠ Families at the End of the Year

Dusting the Eaves: In Suzhou, whether it's a small family or a large household, at the end of each year, they must first have a thorough cleaning of the dust in the house. From the beams to the corners of the walls, everything is cleaned, called "Dusting the Eaves." There is a saying in Suzhou, "Before accomplishing anything, first dust the eaves," because dusting the eaves is the first task of passing the year. The days are chosen according to the water days on the almanac, taking the meaning of avoiding fire. Sending off the Kitchen God and Thanking the Year: Eating is indeed a major difficulty in life! Therefore, the Kitchen God, who governs the kitchen, receives the highest respect from old families. On the 23rd and 24th days of the lunar year, it is the day for the Kitchen God to ascend to Heaven to report the good and bad deeds of each family. In Suzhou, on these two days, every family prepares paper sedan chairs, sets up vegetarian feasts, and respectfully sends off the Kitchen God to Heaven. On the feast for sending off the Kitchen God, a candy ingot must be offered. The Kitchen God, after eating the sweet treat, will only say good things when reporting. This ridiculous superstitious act is still preserved in Suzhou society. As for thanking the year, it involves preparing chicken, fish, and three kinds of sacrifices, offering them to the gods to express gratitude. The date for thanking the year is either fixed every year or chosen according to an auspicious day on the almanac. The scroll with the image of the gods is also hung in the hall on the day of thanking the year.

New Year's Eve Dinner: After worshiping the ancestors, the full dishes invite relatives and friends, surrounding family members, and enjoying the feast. During the feast, dishes are passed around, and auspicious words are spoken. For example, fish is said to mean "abundance," bamboo shoots mean "rising steadily," shrimp mean "smooth sailing," chicken means "growing vigorously," oranges mean "round fortune," vermicelli means "golden chains," and green fruits, ark clams, egg dumplings, etc., are all commonly called "earning ingots." And at the bottom of each bowl of rice, a cooked water chestnut is hidden, called digging for treasure, meaning digging for hidden wealth. The meal is eaten at night, called New Year's Eve Dinner.

Sealing the Well and Welcoming the Kitchen God: On Lunar New Year's Eve, every family, because the old Kitchen God has ascended to Heaven and the kitchen cannot be vacant forever, the new Kitchen God takes office at the end of the year. At the same time, the well is sealed, and the Well Spring Boy, who represents water (homophone for power), is worshiped. Then, firecrackers are set off to seal the door, carrying out the ancient saying "With the sound of firecrackers, the old is removed."

㈡ Society at the End of the Year

Storytelling Sessions: Storytelling is Suzhou people's specialty of "speaking with a single mouth." Ma Rufei and Liu Jingting were certainly well-known figures in the past, and Guangyu Society is also a powerful modern folk organization in Suzhou. Storytelling sessions take place at the end of each year. At each storytelling venue, four or five storytellers take turns performing. The stories told at the sessions emphasize humor. If a storyteller is good, the listeners laugh heartily, and their reputation spreads by word of mouth. But those with poor elocution, due to the number of people telling stories at the sessions, often face the embarrassment of being booed off the stage, so many are not counted. As for the proceeds from the sessions, the storytellers only take 200 copper coins. Half of the remainder goes to the teahouses, and the other half goes to the annual expenses of the Storytelling Association and Yucai Elementary School.

Sending Ingots: When the teahouses and bathhouses reach the end of the year, the waiters send a small bag of olives and a few oranges, called sending ingots, to their regular customers. The recipient must give at least one yuan in return. At the same time, the prices at bathhouses and barbershops double after the 24th, compared to normal days.

Odds and Ends: At the end of the year, the rice cake and tea snack shops pile up rice cakes like small mountains, and nandina and wintersweet are also sold as New Year's offerings. Groups of beggars dress up as turtles and yellow cattle, going around the streets begging for money. Under the electric lights on New Year's Eve, people can still be found carrying lanterns, collecting debts.

Free Talk

The Front Line 212

— Zhu Wen

Written for the Anniversary of the January 28 Incident

The enemy's prepared second general offensive is about to erupt in a day or two. The situation has become even more serious. The new commander-in-chief sent from Tokyo has also arrived. The naval landing forces, which were boasted about in peacetime, are now suffering unexpected blows from the Chinese troops every day and have increased many elite land forces. Every day, countless stories are heard of Japanese soldiers massacring Chinese civilians. Several hundred people were captured, imprisoned in houses, and whipped, some starving while being forced to do hard labor for them.

Recently, it has become even more difficult to walk on the roads. San De and his friends can no longer risk selling newspapers every day to earn a few copper coins. They have already discussed with the familiar soldiers nearby that as long as each of them gets the firearms and other items of the brothers who died on the spot, they can stand on the front line and fight alongside the troops. At this moment, they can't care about the roster and other things, aiming their guns at the imperialists is all that matters.

San De, Dafa, and Agen learned that there probably wouldn't be any battles on this road tonight, so they joined the team at dusk and really found an opportunity to get everything sorted out with their familiar friends. About half of this group of people have been injured or killed since the beginning of the war. Every face shows signs of exhaustion, but they are still excited and energetic. They only sleep for two or three hours a day, but no one says they are tired. They immediately wake up as soon as they hear the enemy's gunfire.

Several partners taught them how to load and fire the guns and also taught them the experience of how to throw grenades.

"Killing people is so easy!" Zhou Sanbao said with a smile.

"Killing people is easy, but orders are not easy. We only hear about Japanese imperialists issuing general attack orders one after another, but it's really difficult for us to get an attack order! When we encircled the enemy the day before yesterday, we could have messed them up completely, but we were ordered not to rush over, right Lao Zhou? The regimental commander was also a little angry, but he knew that it wouldn't work if the brothers under him made a fuss, and in the end, he would still suffer from the higher-ups, so he learned his lesson last time and obeyed the order. We really hate it. The enemy that was clearly surrounded was so anxious that they couldn't think of a way, their left wing suffered such a big loss, and the whole army would be panicked, but we let them go so easily!"

"We later asked the regimental commander in private, and he had to say that it was because of the overall military plan, and there was no way to think about it. Damn it!"

It was quite dark before dinner was delivered.

"Hey, Wang Baolin, why is dinner delivered so late? How many meals do you eat a day?" Dafa asked the flat-faced man next to him. His stomach, which had been hungry for two days, grumbled especially loudly when he saw the rice.

"They're afraid to send it during the day because of the planes. We eat dinner at this time, and breakfast will be delivered before dawn."

Everyone filled their bowls tightly and quickly swallowed the rice with a little bit of vegetables. Just as everyone was eating their second bowl, the sound of rifles and machine guns clearly erupted. The three of them, who had just stepped onto the front line, immediately stopped eating and asked their other partners. Zhou Sanbao told them that the sound wasn't from the enemy in front of them and that it wasn't a formal battle either. This kind of situation often happens, but it's just the enemy testing the waters.

Not long after dinner, because they expected that there wouldn't be much fighting tonight and they were preparing to deal with the second general offensive that was coming soon, the company commander ordered everyone to go to bed early. (To be continued)

"Rationalizing Escape" 213

— He Jiagan

In ancient times, being a woman was terribly unlucky. Every move was wrong, this was scolded, that was scolded. Now, this misfortune has fallen on the students' heads. Advancing is scolded, retreating is scolded.

We still remember how the students stirred up trouble since the winter of the year before last. Some wanted to go south, some wanted to go north. They were not allowed to board the trains going south or north. By the time they reached the capital and petitioned on their knees, they unexpectedly were "used by the reactionaries." Many heads happened to "bump" into bayonets and rifle butts, and some even "accidentally fell into the water" and died.

Who dared to raise a protest? Some people even laughed and scolded them.

They were also expelled, their parents were notified, and they were urged to advance to the research institutes. A year has passed, and finally things have quieted down. But unexpectedly, Shanhaiguan has fallen. Shanghai is still far away, but Beiping is no longer safe because even the research institutes are in danger. People living in Shanghai must remember, could they still sit in the research institutes of Jinan University and Labor University on this day last year?

The university students in Beiping know this, and they have a good memory. This time, they no longer use their heads to "bump" into bayonets and rifle butts, nor do they want to "accidentally fall into the water." Instead, they invented a new method, which is to scatter and go home.

This is precisely the effect of the education in recent years.

But then again, someone came to scold them. The Boy Scouts are still in the elegies of the martyrs, saying that they "leave a stench for ten thousand years."

But let us think about it: aren't even the inanimate antiques in the Institute of Linguistics and History being moved? Isn't it true that students cannot each have an airplane? Can those who can get dazed from bumping into native bayonets and rifle butts and hide in the research institutes be unaffected by the foreign airplanes and cannons bombing them out of the research institutes?

Amitabha!

Orchids and Pekingese 214

— Cao Juren

｜Speaking at the Shanghai Literary and Art Tea Party｜

Distinguished gentlemen and ladies:

Mr. ×× wants me to talk about my views on literature and art! Literature and art are such noble things that we country folk cannot talk about them.

Just now, Mr. Sun Fuxi talked about plum blossoms and then orchids, saying that orchids grow in deep mountains and that their fragrance moves people, saying how those who pick orchids cut through thorns, enter deep valleys, climb dangerous cliffs, and face all kinds of hardships before they can pick them, saying how beauties and fragrant herbs are praised in the poems of ancient and modern scholars, and also talking about the orchids' solitary appreciation of their own beauty, as noble as the artists and writers who love beauty.

I am sorry! We country folk didn't know that orchids were so noble. Just a hundred steps from my house, on a low mountain ridge, there are many orchids in those thatched nests. They are picked in handfuls and baskets. In the time it takes to burn a stick of incense, dozens of plants can be found. I never entered any deep valleys or climbed any dangerous cliffs. Twenty years ago, when I was studying in Jinhua, I saw orchids being sold for 240 cash per load and found it very strange. Who knew that orchids had such a noble status? I am truly very sorry!

After praising plum blossoms, you have to praise orchids. After praising orchids, you have to praise peonies and herbaceous peonies. Artists and writers in spring are truly as busy as a thousand or ten thousand every day! We country folk, after seeing the rapeseed flowers, the azaleas on the mountains are blooming vigorously, filling the mountains and valleys, one after another, and there are always thirty days to see. After seeing the azaleas, the clover flowers fill the fields, and they are also very lively. Spring is a busy time for farm work, and there is never time to praise them, but they still bloom vigorously every year!

I heard that in wealthy families in the city, they always raise three or five Pekingese, and in front of the steps, they always place a few pots of orchids. This is indeed a well-matched pairing, winning the hearts of young ladies, young masters, masters, and madams.

Please forgive us country folk for not understanding the merits of these two noble treasures.

Shrimp, Eel, and Others 215

— Peng Jiahuang

All living beings have their own ways of life and instincts to resist external aggression. Some fight with horns, tigers and leopards with claws and teeth, mules and horses with hooves, and those without weapons rely on protection to avoid enemy attacks. For example, cabbage worms are all green, hiding in cabbage leaves, making it difficult for enemies to detect them. Like cuttlefish, when they sense a life-threatening danger, they eject ink, hiding in the ink, making it difficult for enemies to recognize them. Other, weaker lower organisms rely on great reproductive power to maintain the continuation of the race, such as mayflies, bedbugs, and lice. Although they live in the morning and die in the evening, although they are constantly captured by people, they always have the opportunity to coexist and prosper with humans!

I remember it was the Mid-Autumn Festival last year when my wife bought shrimp and eel. At that time, I was in Ningbo, which was not suffering from any "national crisis", and I thought that the shrimp and eel in Ningbo would also be free from "national crisis." Originally, humans are strong, the kings of animals, eating pork, eating beef, killing chickens and cooking lamb—these are common occurrences. I was also bored and paid attention to these animals, which would soon enter my mouth. The shrimp jumped in the basket, then squirmed in the bucket. I thought, no matter how much they jumped and twisted, since they had been caught and bought from the fishmonger, they would not survive, and this jumping and twisting was obviously meaningless. However, even though they are small creatures destined to die, in this time of crisis and survival, they always know to jump and twist, making their enemies who kill them spend more effort and feel annoyed and bothered!

Shrimp can only jump clumsily and are relatively easy to deal with, so I only paid attention to how my wife killed the eel. She was an amateur at killing eel. She had no way to catch the slippery eel. She wanted to scald them to death with boiling water and then cut them open. I said this method of killing was too stupid, and there would be no fresh, bloody taste when eating it. She wanted to flatten the eel's head so that there would be blood and freshness, but as she hit it, the eel slipped and danced like a dragon or snake. I told her, "Why don't you anesthetize the eel with wine!" Sure enough, when the wine was poured into the bucket, the eel's mouth moved a few times, and then it looked like it was dead. After a while, all these animals were taken care of. I laughed at my wife, "Haha, you're also a third-rate imperialist!"

I used to kill eel in the countryside, which was done by brute force. I would just grab its head, make a cut from the side of its head with small scissors, break open its belly, and pull out its intestines. But even without its internal organs, the animal would still struggle. I also killed frogs, cut off their heads, skinned them, cut off their limbs, opened their bellies, and took out their livers and lungs, but when thrown into a basin of water, they could still jump and swim. However, it was strange to have actions without painful cries! In short, for such animals to struggle so hard when there is no need to struggle is really too stupid and meaningless!

After all, humans, especially humans from the land of China, are more refined and intelligent. Before being caught and skinned, they don't jump or twist, and they lead each other, refraining from jumping or twisting together. After the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, the anniversaries had long passed, and amidst "having our own ways" of "long-term resistance" and "psychological resistance," the enemy had invaded Shanhaiguan. Although fierce bombs were thrown at the hot-blooded youth who were good at picking and twisting, they still did not jump or twist. Because what's the use? What's the meaning? Sooner or later, they will be skinned like shrimp and eel! Besides, it was investigated clearly ten years ago that there are 450 million humans in the land of China. You can skin them as you please. With our great reproductive power, we won't be wiped out in three to five years.

Shenbao Medical Weekly

Medical Experience and Experimentation 217

— Song Guobin

The word "experience" occupies an important position in Chinese social thought. Speaking requires experience, doing things requires experience, and emphasizing experience over experimentation has almost become a characteristic of the Chinese people!

Experience and truth go hand in hand. Experience derived from truth is most worthy of cherishing, but experience that is unrelated to or even contrary to truth is not only useless but also harmful! It should be understood that experience is not a bad thing in itself; its benefits or harms depend entirely on whether the user uses it well. Does medicine not value experience? The foundation of medicine is built on science, and the first principle of science is experimentation. Truth is the crystallization of experimentation, and the experience of new medicine is based on experimentation. It can also be said that it is the experience of truth. For example, experience tells us it is like this, but what is the result of experimentation? It is something else entirely, and then we immediately know that the report of experience is completely wrong! Old medicine has two types of experience: one is based on predecessors, and the other belongs to oneself. What medicine to use for what disease, predecessors did it this way, and later generations can do it this way too. Predecessors obtained it from experience, and the experience of predecessors, left to later generations, becomes truth. Later generations only know to silently adhere to the truth derived from the experience of predecessors, without asking whether this principle is true or not. This is the secret of old medicine's treatment of diseases—it is also the biggest reason why old medicine has remained unchanged for thousands of years in China. A's disease was cured like this, B's disease is the same as A's, so use the same treatment method. Day after day, the more similar diseases seen, the richer the experience becomes. But the reason why this treatment is necessary is never known. And thus, a strange phenomenon arises: what A doctor diagnoses is like this, what B doctor diagnoses is like that—what is the reason? It is because the methods they use are entirely based on experience. A doctor's experience is like this, B doctor's experience is like that, and the difference in treatment is the result of their experience. If we use experimental methods to examine and determine their right and wrong, perhaps we can say that both are wrong. This is one's own experience.

The condition of illness is ever-changing, and there are many cases of the same symptoms with different causes. A slight difference can lead to a great error. Experience can only tell us the generalities of the disease, but not what exactly the disease is or why it needs to be treated this way. Therefore, from experience, we can obtain a general range, and then conduct experiments in this direction to obtain truth. Compared to someone without experience conducting experiments, it can save time and energy. Conversely, if we rely solely on experience without conducting experiments, then at least some of this experience is unreliable, and using it to treat diseases is certainly dangerous.

My conclusion is that medicine is objective, and medical experience must be supplemented by experimentation. Experience derived from experimentation is truth.

Common Knowledge Question and Answer on Diseases 218

— Cheng Hanzhang

(2) Influenza

Q: What is called influenza?

A: This is a very common infectious disease. Because the symptoms that appear are mostly the same as ordinary colds, but it often spreads widely, it is called influenza. But the actual confirmation may not be reliable.

Q: What is the Western name for influenza?

A: The Western names are Influenza or LaGrippe.

Q: In which year was this disease very widespread?

A: In 1918-20, there was a worldwide epidemic, which was then specifically called the Spanish Flu (Spanish Grippe).

Q: Is this disease found every year?

A: Yes, there are small local epidemics every winter.

Q: Can people who have had this disease become immune?

A: Although there is immunity, it is very short-lived, only about one or two months.

Q: What is the pathogen of influenza?

A: It is the influenza bacillus discovered by Pfeiffer. However, when the disease occurs, there are often mixed infections of pneumococci, staphylococci, streptococci, and Triedlander's bacilli.

Q: Which part of the body does the pathogen infect first?

A: It first infects the nasal passages and throat.

Q: How many days after being infected with this pathogen does the disease develop?

A: The disease develops in one to three days.

Q: When the disease develops, what are the most common first symptoms?

A: Sudden chills, fever, general fatigue, headache, forehead pain, limb pain, low back pain, etc.

Q: What are the later symptoms?

A: Usually, it is the mucosal inflammation type, mainly involving the respiratory system. That is, rhinitis, laryngitis, pharyngitis, and tracheobronchitis. There is nasal discharge, throat pain, hoarseness, and coughing. There is compressive pain above and below the eye sockets.

Q: Is there a fever?

A: Yes, there is a fever. But the fever type is not fixed, usually between 39 and 40 degrees Celsius.

Q: Are there more dangerous symptoms?

A: There is a type that progresses very quickly, with a sudden rise in body temperature, rapid pulse, mental confusion, and can be fatal after three or four days. It is called fulminant influenza.

Q: Are there other types of the disease?

A: There are several other types. One is called the toxic type, which occurs about two or three weeks later, with another high fever leading to exhaustion. There is also a type that invades the lungs, called the pulmonary type, causing pneumonia. There is also a type that invades the gastrointestinal tract, called the gastrointestinal type, causing vomiting, diarrhea, bloody stools, and abdominal pain. Even more, there is a type that invades the nervous system, called the nervous type, causing encephalitis, meningitis, neuritis, and mental illness.

Q: Are there other complications in patients with influenza?

A: There are complications of conjunctivitis, otitis media, nephritis, pericarditis, peribronchitis, and sinus empyema.

Q: What is the treatment for this disease?

A: In the early stages of the disease, take diaphoretic drugs, such as aspirin, antipyrene, and phenacetin. In cases of sepsis, colloidal silver solution can be injected, or 606, etc. As for symptomatic treatment, take expectorants, cardiotonics, antitussives, and sedatives. Warm and moist compresses or anti-inflammatory clay poultices can be applied to the chest. If there is sinus empyema, surgical incision may be necessary.

The Problem of Lung Disease in China (Continued) 219

— Ding Huikang

(1) The Importance of Early Diagnosis and the Results of Early Treatment

Although tuberculosis is a dreadful disease, if it can be diagnosed early and treated appropriately, there is no risk of it not being cured. However, in the early stages of the disease, people often do not pay close attention to it, and may even neglect it. When fever, hemoptysis, and other symptoms occur, they become flustered and confused. Although treatment may stop the fever and bleeding, they think that the disease is cured. However, tuberculosis is a chronic disease, and fever and hemoptysis are only one type or temporary phenomenon in the disease. Even if they occasionally subside, it does not mean that the disease is cured. Without the guidance of a doctor, without seeking to cultivate the body and increase resistance, the root of the disease will lie dormant, and the disease will eventually erupt one day, falling into a severe state. At this time, seeking medical attention is not entirely dependent on the power of medicine, and the proper treatment period has been lost, which is regrettable.

The three stages of tuberculosis: The first is the latent period, which lasts from the time the tubercle bacillus invades the human body until the symptoms appear. The time can range from several months to one or two years, depending on each person's resistance and environment. The second is the symptomatic period, the length of which is uncertain, with some developing danger in a few days and others lasting for decades. The third is the early recovery period, which is when the patient has undergone treatment, has no subjective symptoms, and gradually recovers health.

If we can diagnose lung disease during its latent period and administer appropriate treatment, the results will be twice as effective with half the effort, avoiding the appearance of symptoms. However, diagnosis is quite difficult during the latent period, and patients are also unaware that they are ill, so there is no way to seek medical examination. Therefore, preparing for diagnosis during the latent period cannot be realized today. What we should pay attention to is

The early signs of tuberculosis: If your weight is gradually decreasing, you often feel tired when working, and coughing continues for one or two months or more, sometimes improving and sometimes recurring, and does not stop, or your appetite is poor, digestion is bad, or you have a slight fever in the afternoon, cold sweats on your chest or back when you wake up at night, or a small amount of blood streaks in your sputum, or coughing is worse in the morning and evening, and you cough up phlegm early in the morning, then you must immediately ask a doctor to examine your body to see if you have lung disease. At this time, the most important thing to avoid is neglecting the importance of X-rays and the discovery of early infiltration. Early diagnosis of lung disease is the first problem to be solved in the treatment of lung disease. However, in the early stages of the disease, the symptoms are extremely subtle. If we use the old Chinese diagnostic methods, such as "observation, inquiry, auscultation, and palpation" to make an accurate diagnosis, it is impossible. The clever ones often write the four words "beware of lung disease" in the pulse record, just to fulfill their responsibility. In addition, examining sputum and using auscultation and percussion, the results obtained are also extremely subtle. If tubercle bacilli are found in the sputum examination, and various rales are heard in auscultation, and dullness is present in percussion, then the patient is already in a serious state. It is not the early infiltration period, and the proper treatment period has been lost. Therefore, to discover early infiltration early, that is, early diagnosis of lung disease, it is necessary to use X-ray photography. At this time, shadows of unequal size can be revealed. Not only is it convenient for doctors to treat, but the patient can also be alerted to take preventive measures and seek medical attention early. In one fell swoop, several good things are achieved. Furthermore, if the X-ray does not show any signs of lung disease, it is even more gratifying. Not only is it unnecessary to seek medical attention, but there are also benefits in terms of economics and time, and the body and mind are also more pleasant.

In short, lung disease cannot detect the existence or absence of early infiltration by relying solely on percussion and auscultation. Before the development of science, most patients with lung disease lost the most suitable time for treatment, leading to rampant lung disease and becoming a great enemy of mankind. If ways can be found to diagnose early infiltration, then lung disease has a great tendency to be cured. Therefore, those who are at risk of contracting lung disease, or whose family and friends have lung disease, or those who are physically weak, if they often feel a slight fever, feverish palms, physical discomfort, coughing, etc., should immediately undergo an X-ray examination to clarify the cause of the disease. Then, there will be great progress in the prevention and treatment of lung disease, and with early treatment, lung disease can certainly be cured, so lung disease is truly not to be feared. What is to be feared is that patients lack the knowledge of the importance of early diagnosis, and generally delay and procrastinate until the disease progresses, and then throw medicine haphazardly, resulting in the loss of the proper treatment period, which is regrettable.

Readers, please be aware that if you encounter someone suspected of having lung disease, you should advise them to seek diagnosis immediately. You must know that with early treatment, not only can physical health be restored early, but the economy of money and time is also a trivial matter. Since I have served in the hospital, I have seen that most of the patients' illnesses are due to the carelessness of early treatment. There are those who regret it for the rest of their lives, those who leave harm to their wives and children, and the losses to society and the country are even more obvious. The sights are shocking and heartbreaking, and nothing is worse than this. Therefore, I cannot help but speak earnestly. May those in the world who care do not disregard these words.

Lung Disease and Taking Medicine

Patients with tuberculosis who exclusively believe in medicine will never hope to be cured. Because there are two types of drugs, one is a drug with special effects, and the other is a drug that is generally symptomatic. At present, "there is no specific drug" for tuberculosis has been found. The drugs taken are mostly of a general nature, such as those that relieve coughs and dissolve phlegm, stimulate the appetite and nourish the blood, stop sweating, and strengthen the body. Therefore, in the early stages of the disease, if there is no guidance from a specialist doctor, but only seeking so-called sacred drugs and special drugs for tuberculosis and taking them, it is like heading south by driving the chariot north. I have not seen it work. Moreover, the so-called various sacred drugs and special drugs are not seen in countries with developed science, but in our country with backward science, they are dazzling and eye-catching. The number of colorful tuberculosis drugs is difficult to count. In reality, it only suffers the common people who have no medical knowledge. In the early stages of the disease, there is an opportunity to be cured, but because they do not know the importance of isolation and recuperation, they exclusively beg for medicine and repeatedly delay until the disease becomes serious before seeking medical attention, and it is too late. However, are drugs really ineffective for lung disease? This cannot be

Page 20

generalized. In general, drugs formally prescribed by a doctor can indirectly increase resistance for the sick body, but they cannot directly eradicate tubercle bacilli.

In short, drugs for tuberculosis may be effective at the time, but they cannot eradicate the bacteria and fundamentally solve the problem, and recurrence is inevitable in the future. Dr. Miller, director of the Shanghai Sanitarium, said that tuberculosis patients who believe in medicine are better off being content with their fate and getting close to nature. But I believe that natural recuperation is a great help for treating the lungs, but it is limited to mild illnesses. Those with early cavities must first find ways to remove the lesions, and then supplement with long-term recuperation to achieve complete success. Therefore, patients should not quickly believe in medicine, nor should they exclusively rely on natural recuperation. They must have a deep determination, get rid of all worldly affairs, strictly rest, and receive specialized treatment, so that the root of the disease can be eradicated, recovery can be expected, and the gift of health can be restored. (To be continued)

Chinese Medicine Used in a Western Way (Continued) 220

— Zhou Mengbai

(4) Asafoetida

Origin

This product is the rootstock of HoruleAsafoetidaLinne and FerulafoetidaRegal or other Ferula plants of the Umbejjiferae family, which is cut and boiled to extract a resin containing gum.

Shape

This product has a few granular ones, called granular asafoetida (Asafoetidainganis), which is of good quality. The medicinal ones are harvested from this type. There are also giant block ones, called block asafoetida (Asafoetidainmassa), which is not a pure product and is not harvested for medicinal purposes. The fresh product has a white broken surface, gradually showing a red iridescence, and then turns yellowish or brownish. The dry quality is brittle, hard, and easily broken. It has a garlic-like odor, a harsh and bitter taste. When heated, it releases a good, fast aroma.

Ingredients

Granular asafoetida contains about 61% ferulic acid (Ferulasaure), other resins, gums, vanillin, volatile oils, etc. The reason why asafoetida has a foul odor is that its volatile oil contains sulfur.

Experimentation

One gram of this product, three milliliters of distilled water, grind it, and you should get a whitish emulsion. Add

a small amount of starch solution, which will turn yellow. Also, add one gram of this product to 10 ml of petroleum benzene, grind for 12 hours, filter, add 10 ml of freshly prepared copper acetate solution to the filtrate, shake and let stand. The petroleum benzene layer should not be dyed green. If it is green, it is proof that it is mixed with rosin.

Efficacy

This product is an antispasmodic, used for hysteria, pertussis, spasm, etc. Take 0.2 to 1.0 several times a day. It is also used as an enema material to expel pinworms.

Storage

This product should be placed in a tin can containing quicklime.

(Appendix Old Theory) Spicy, calm, enters the spleen and stomach, eliminates meat accumulation, kills small insects, removes odor, resolves toxins from rapeseed and dead cattle and horses, treats cold pain in the heart and abdomen, malaria, dysentery, infectious diseases, malnutrition, ghosts, and venom. Now, the medicine shops fill it with fried garlic cloves, so it is necessary to distinguish it.

Scientific Childbearing (4) 221

— Yu Songyun

(7) Accurate Diagnosis of Pregnancy

The diagnosis of whether or not one is pregnant is most difficult to determine in the first one or two months. Our famous traditional Chinese medicine practitioners can often determine whether or not one is pregnant based on the pulse record. Some traditional Chinese medicine practitioners say that a 50-day-old fetus can also be diagnosed on the pulse. This statement is a bit too ridiculous. Now I will write down the various diagnostic methods in detail, hoping that readers will pay attention to them.

(A) Accurate Diagnostic Method

To accurately diagnose pregnancy, a detailed examination of the uterus must be performed, or a chemical test, or palpation and listening to fetal heart sounds, etc.

(1) Uterine examination: If fertilization has occurred, the size of the uterus increases monthly, and the fundus of the uterus has a certain position, which is detailed in the previous article.

(2) Palpation: Divided into internal and external methods. External palpation method: Place your hand flat on the convex part of the abdomen and massage slowly to test for fetal movement. The larger the number of months, the easier it is to check. Internal palpation method: Make the pregnant woman lie on her back, insert one finger into the vagina, and place the other hand on the fundus of the uterus. Push one finger in the vagina upward to the cervix to feel the size of the uterus, and compare it with the number of months since menstruation stopped.

(3) Fetal heart sound: After 20 weeks of pregnancy, the fetal heart sound can be heard. Listening to fetal heart sounds in the second half of pregnancy is very obvious.

If any one of the above several methods can be determined, it can prove certainty.

(Note) Pregnancy is a physiological phenomenon in a woman, not a disease, but it can also be affected by it, so that it is easy to contract diseases. (To be continued)

(6) Salts

Most Foods and Drinks Contain Green Salts and Mineral Salts, etc.

(7) Water Content

All Fresh Foods and Drinks, as well as those Cooked, Contain a Large Amount of Water, Except for Dry or Dried Products, Which Contain Very Little.

2. Suitable Nutritional Methods

A. Complete Nutritional Foods: The three main elements in foods should be included in the daily nutrition, and various foods should be combined. If using foods that lean towards one element, then the other two are lacking, or if two are lacking, then one is lacking, which often leads to malnutrition.

B. Mainly Plant-Based Foods: Our daily foods are usually a mix of animal and plant-based foods. As seen above, vitamins are abundant in various plants. However, proteins and fats cannot be omitted either, but using a small amount is enough to supplement them. Therefore, using mainly plant-based foods for nutrition is still sound, as seen in Eastern nations. As for foods, fresh and living ones are the best.

C. Good Fats and Oils: Animal fats such as fresh cream, cod liver oil, and various extracted vegetable oils such as olive oil, peanut oil, rapeseed oil, tea oil, sesame oil, soybean oil, etc., are good because they greatly increase the secretion of digestive juices, such as gastric juice, bile, pancreatic juice, etc., and indirectly stimulate intestinal peristalsis, which is beneficial for promoting nutrition. However, heated and processed fats are not easily digested, and using them may cause indigestion in the stomach and intestines. All animal and plant fats and oils should be freshly made. Moreover, long-stored ones are often spoiled or have various preservatives added, which is very bad.

D. Introduce Large Amounts of Vitamins into the Body: Fresh plant foods are very rich in vitamins. Refer to the various food items. If using many processed foods, the ingredients in them may be completely lost or only a small amount remains. Therefore, it is advisable to eat more fresh foods, such as vegetables and fruits. Vitamin B is the easiest to lose, so unrefined rice and wheat, as well as other foods rich in Vitamin B, should be consumed daily to avoid a deficiency of this vitamin, which can cause beriberi.

E. No Need to Drink Too Much Water Daily: The foods consumed daily already contain a large amount of water, which is enough for the body. Drinking too much water will dilute the digestive juices in the stomach and cause them to accumulate inside, also causing the stomach to swell, leading to indigestion and gastrectasia. Summer and after sweating are exceptions. As for drinking water, it is not easily absorbed; however, orange and lemon juice are more easily absorbed and provide a quick feeling of quenching thirst and coolness.

F. Daily Food Intake Should Not Be Excessive: When healthy, consuming only 90% of one's appetite is sufficient for the body's needs. Excessive consumption is also wasteful and overworks the stomach and intestines, causing them to be injured. The various functions of the entire body are also overworked, leading to premature aging.

G. Meal Times: In addition to following local customs and family habits, the following points should also be noted:

1. It is advisable to rest a little before eating in order to eat properly.

2. It is advisable to change the environment during meals and temporarily forget work.

3. Meal times should be ample in order to chew thoroughly; rapid swallowing is harmful to the stomach.

4. Rest for one hour after eating before engaging in mental or physical labor; otherwise, blood flow to the internal organs will be reduced, which will also harm digestion.

8. Nutritional Foods and Addictions to Avoid: A. Tobacco and Alcohol, Because addiction harms the body.

B. Coffee, Tea, and Leaf Tea, These types of tea also contain stimulating substances, and addiction harms the body.

C. Salt: We use it to season food, but it is often used to stimulate the kidneys, which may harm the kidneys and easily lead to gallstones and kidney stones. It is advisable to reduce or avoid it, but the body will not be deficient because most foods contain green salt, and input is already rich, so there is no harm.

D. Spices and Other Stimulating Substances in Soups: Soups, braised meats, and crispy foods contain spices and stimulating substances, which make them very delicious and can stimulate the appetite, but prolonged use can harm the stomach, leading to poor appetite and indigestion.

Discussions

How to Commemorate January 28th 223

— Shen

January 28th. With a heart full of fervent grief, I "calmly" walked onto the streets amidst the cheerful clamor of "Happy New Year," because I also "loved my country and did not lag behind," and had already "prepared for long-term resistance." So, besides "saving the country with my conscience" and not buying inferior goods, I also wanted to see if our "patriotic heroes" were as enthusiastic as I was. Perhaps I would be lucky enough to witness some earth-shattering events, but I was very disappointed. It was no different than usual. Many shops were only displaying Spring Festival couplets to mark the "market strike" in mourning.

Helpless, I bought a special edition of the newspaper on that day.

In this half sheet of newspaper, I gained many satisfying lessons. I carefully copied the newspaper as follows:

⊙ Yokosuka: On the 28th, to commemorate the first anniversary of the Shanghai Incident, the Yokosuka Gunnery School, under the command of former Major General Sha, held a simulated street battle to recall the incident. (Report from the 27th, Dentsu Agency)

(Nanjing) Various circles in the capital decided to hold a commemorative meeting for the first anniversary of the January 28th Anti-Japanese War at the National Grand Theater at 9:00 AM on the 28th, with Zhang Yuanliang (note, not Zhang Xueliang) as the chairman. All citizens observed one minute of silence (of course, not three minutes) at 11:00 AM to express their condolences, and drafted commemorative slogans and many major proposals. (Report from the 27th, Central News Agency)

After reading these two messages in comparison, alas, I want to remain silent. Fortunately, the same newspaper also has an article that is exciting enough, and of course, there is a need to spread it. I hope you will not regard it lightly.

"…Therefore, we can only recognize the reasons for the outbreak of the January 28th disaster if we clearly recognize the increasingly profound and expanded active aggression of Japanese imperialism. At the same time, we can only recognize the current way out for our nation if we grasp the theory of answering the war of aggression by Japanese imperialism with a national revolutionary war.

····································

The January 28th bloody battle is glorious. In the history of national revolution, it will always be one of the most valuable contributions. However, in terms of the current situation of our nation, this glorious war should not stop with January 28th.

…We can commemorate January 28th, not with tears, not with sighs, not with sorrow, but with blood. We should strengthen our own bulwarks, should recognize the current great enemy, and should firmly grasp the weapon of national revolutionary war. Only in this way can we maintain the glory of the January 28th Anti-Japanese bloody battle, and only in this way can we promote our nation towards a world of bright future."

Arts and Literature

Leaving the Country, Song of Famous Pass 224

— Qi Yu

Riding the Cang Dragon north, I gaze at the imperial capital in Liaodong, soaring majestically to the ninth heaven, embracing the peaks of Hebei, like fierce beasts crouching on all sides, and like playful divine dragons. Hundreds of streams vie to wash its feet, and the hills and mounds come to offer homage. Towering and not vulgar, it is indeed the hero of the universe. The vast Bohai Sea embraces it in front, and the winding Great Wall seals it to the west. Looking east at the boundless plains, the land is rich and its bounty abundant. For a long time, strong neighbors have stealthily watched it, and the majestic pass angrily glares and deters the wicked. Suddenly, chaos erupts overnight, instantly darkening the majestic countenance of the famous fortress. The heavens, the earth, the grass, and the trees all change color, why do these living creatures not beat their chests? I grieve for the soldiers who give their lives while the main generals are cowardly and timid, the epitome of eternal foolishness. People also whisper their words, but they turn a deaf ear to them. Righteous armies suddenly rise beyond the border, and the masses proclaim, "We vow to provide support!" But why are there so many mouths and so few hands in this world, only hearing empty words of saving the country? I lament the righteous army's bloody battles, while you are embracing prostitutes and drunkenly sleeping. They use guns and cannons, we use blood and flesh, the horizontal division is everywhere, but who pities them?

Ammunition is exhausted, and support is cut off, the sound shakes the sky, and close combat ensues. Cannons are like thunder, and machine guns are like bees, heads are suddenly severed, and limbs are quickly broken. The wind howls, piercingly cold, the sky is bleak, and snow falls again. The desert is vast, and the air is gloomy, and rivers freeze for thousands of miles. Horses neigh, and apes howl, facing the daylight, they suspect ghosts. The country mourns its dead, and freeloaders surrender, the mountains rage, and the seas sob. The famous pass grieves, feeling dizzy, the ancient jade tablet is now a broken stone tablet.

In chaos, it is said, "Being brave in private fights but timid in public is why ancient countries lose their soldiers." Those dignitaries steal joy and are slow and lazy, so the famous pass is abandoned to the east. Gazing at the disordered border clouds from afar, I feel a sense of desolation, and tears fall. My hatred is boundless, how can I bear to end my life like this!

Common Knowledge

Urban Air Defense 225

— Meng Fu

The slogan "No air defense, no national defense" has been clearly verified since the January 28th Shanghai Incident last year. Try to imagine with your eyes closed the bomber soaring five thousand meters above the ground, carrying large bombs weighing up to a ton or thousands of fierce incendiary bombs, and attacking like a violent storm. The bustling market instantly turns into scorched earth. It's enough to make one shudder. Now, enemy planes are rampant in the Rehe-Shanhaiguan area, and the air defense problem is really pressing.

The so-called "air defense" can also be said to be urban air defense, because the target that the enemy wants to destroy is the political and economic center of the opposing country, which is the large city. Now, let's briefly describe the urban air defense methods as follows...

(A) Directly Implemented Air Defense Methods

(1) Air Defense Aviation Corps: This organization is the main body of air defense, composed of fighter planes. When enemy planes attack, it is difficult to achieve full effectiveness by only relying on ground-based anti-aircraft guns. The so-called "fighting poison with poison" means that fighter planes must be used to intercept the enemy planes, so that the enemy planes cannot pass through and reach the city at all. Even if they have invaded, they can be annihilated by the fastest means, so that they can suffer less damage. Our country has suffered a lot because it does not have this kind of organization and preparation at all.

(2) Anti-Aircraft Gun Teams and Anti-Aircraft Machine Gun Teams: These two organizations are also the main components of air defense. New-style anti-aircraft guns are effective at six thousand meters above and below, no matter what. Although they cannot completely shoot down enemy planes, they at least give the enemy a kind of intimidation, so that their aerial movements cannot be carried out as they wish. It is best to set up gun positions on dangerous terrain eight thousand meters away from the city, which is tantamount to building an invisible aerial fence for this city. The main purpose of anti-aircraft machine guns is to directly protect buildings or other objects outside the anti-aircraft gun positions, and low-altitude shooting below two thousand meters cannot be done without them.

(3) Barrage Balloon Teams: This method was first used by Germany in the European War, and then Britain and France also followed suit, and the results were very good. Its purpose is to make the balloon collide with the plane, so that all the ropes on the balloon are wrapped around various parts of the fuselage, causing the plane to lose its lift and fall. Although it directly causes very few planes to fall, it at least prevents planes from flying at low altitudes of three thousand meters above and below at night, so the indirect effectiveness is very great.

(B) Indirectly Aiding Air Defense

(1) Lighting Control System: Its task is to extinguish the lights in the whole city so that the enemy loses the target for bombing. All the lights in the inner rooms must be strictly guarded to prevent them from leaking outside. Necessary lights, such as the red and green lights at the train station and the street lights on important traffic roads, must also be covered so that the light does not leak upwards. However, the extinction of lights must be implemented in the villages and towns around the city; otherwise, it will clearly tell the enemy that the dark place is the target. Therefore, although this system has a significant effect, it cannot be achieved without careful preparation and consideration.

(2) Searchlights and Listening Devices: If air defense aviation teams or anti-aircraft gun teams are fighting at night, then searchlights and listening devices are absolutely necessary. The candlelight of searchlights is usually between 200,000,000 and 300,000,000, and the range is about ten kilometers. Listening devices can determine the direction from which enemy planes are coming, and then use searchlights to illuminate them, which is effective. In short, the two must be used in conjunction with each other, which is very effective for night combat, especially for anti-aircraft gun teams.

(3) Air Defense Watchtowers: That is, a balloon is floated to about 50 to 200 kilometers above the ground, and people are sent up to monitor closely with telescopes. If they find enemy planes coming from afar, they will immediately report to the air defense headquarters on the ground.

Most of the air defense methods mentioned above are the responsibility of the government's military department. As for the citizens, they should also have some common sense of air defense. A little bit is briefly described below...

(1) Firefighting: It goes without saying that houses in cities are densely packed, and fires will start due to incendiary bombs. The importance of firefighting can also be imagined. Therefore, in addition to quickly organizing more fire brigades, citizens should usually prepare a supply of water, rubber hoses, sand, ash, and various fire extinguishers. No matter how small a fire is, it must be completely extinguished, otherwise it will become a prairie fire.

(2) Poison Prevention and Poison Gas Removal: When those cruel poison gas bombs are dropped, it is necessary to have sufficient preparation in advance. It is best for citizens to have their own absorption canisters. After the poison gas passes through this canister, it is either absorbed or neutralized to become a non-toxic gas. Usually, activated carbon and soda lime are used for this. The residual poison gas on the ground should be treated with neutralizers or removed by ventilation. There are two types of poison prevention devices for indoor and underground structures: the first method is to completely isolate it from the outside world, but it is necessary to prepare a supply of oxygen; the second method is to install poison gas filtration devices at windows and entrances. In short, poison prevention is a very

Page 22

urgent matter; otherwise, death is very likely.

(3) Shelters: Shelters can be built in houses, but they must be extremely strong, because when an armor-piercing bomb is dropped, even the strength of cement can be broken, but piling up thick soil can prevent it in case of emergency. The most important point is that when enemy planes attack, there is no need to panic excessively. Panic makes it easy to mess things up. It is best to hide in the pre-built shelter at home, and if you are outside, find a depression to hide in. This can at least avoid the fragments of bombs flying out. In short, keep your mind calm, and you may be able to escape from death; otherwise, you will only lose your life.

Impressions of New Year's Day 226

— Qing Cen

The New Year's Day here is the just-passed lively Lunar New Year's Day. Although the lunar calendar has become obsolete, the Lunar New Year festival is already a "discarded year." However, because of the deep-rooted customs and concepts that people have had for thousands of years regarding the lunar calendar, most people still use the lunar calendar, so the Lunar New Year festival is still particularly grand. There are still many people who celebrate the Gregorian New Year and then celebrate the Lunar New Year again, and they are very indifferent to the Gregorian New Year, but very enthusiastic about the Lunar New Year. This is a custom and habit of thousands of years, and it is really not easy to transfer it in a short period of time.

Because I wrote a manuscript on New Year's Eve, I didn't go to sleep until three o'clock in the morning, so when I woke up, it was already eleven o'clock. After washing up, I adjusted the room a little, sorted out another manuscript, and hurriedly went out. I looked at the clock on the street and it was already past one o'clock. The shops were all closed. My stomach was very hungry, but where could I buy something to eat? I remembered that Jie Zi had invited me to spend the New Year. Let's go there. I'll find a food shop on the way. I walked north along Rue Luber. Braving the sharp north wind. The weather was gloomy and cold. When I woke up, I saw a very good sun, but it quickly turned into such gloomy and severe weather. I bravely moved forward in the fierce and roaring cold wind, from Rue Luber to Gordon Road.

The streets on New Year's Day were unusually deserted and desolate. Probably because the weather was too gloomy and cold, people were hiding at home to have fun, or sneaking into theaters and amusement parks. Who would be playing wildly on the streets? The shops were all closed, but from the walls and plank walls, I could hear the sounds of sparrows, mahjong, or the shouting and yelling of gambling inside. On the streets I walked, there was almost no shop or house without the sound of gambling. I thought that in this place, the practical function of gambling has mostly become entertainment. Who doesn't want games? Who doesn't want recreation? And in general Chinese society, the only and most convenient thing that can provide games and recreation is gambling. There are all kinds and varieties of gambling tools everywhere, and gambling is also an interesting game with a competitive nature. So, in the New Year, gambling is generally the most interesting game and pastime.

Children were all wearing new clothes of various colors, surrounded by food stalls and toy stalls by the side of the road. Many children were setting off firecrackers. The small firecrackers would "bang" when they were thrown hard on the ground. The children were the happiest, especially in such a grand, lively, and enjoyable New Year.

At street corners and alleys, there seemed to be many more disabled, old, and weak beggars than usual, each with bodily forms that were pitiful, waiting for the people enjoying the New Year to beg from.

I passed Avenue Foch and Chengdu Road and walked to Carter Road. I still hadn't found a place to eat. My stomach was yelling with hunger. Finally, I found a Tangyuan shop on Carter Road and ate four hot Tangyuan to barely satisfy my hunger. After eating the Tangyuan, I felt a lot of heat added to my body and continued to rush into the cold wind.

I moved forward in the flying snowflakes of Gordon Road. From afar, I heard bursts of violent sounds of "Kill, kill..." Because of my experience as a "Qiu Ba student," I knew that it was probably the army practicing bayonet drills. When I got closer, I went to the gate of the "Joint-Stock Company" of the inner and outer yarn factory and saw a team of Japanese soldiers, Japanese marines, wearing body armor and holding guns with bayonets, practicing bayonet drills in the courtyard inside, practicing the white-blade battle of charging and killing. When Chinese people see this scene, their hearts cannot bear it, let alone me, a young man! I was thinking that today is New Year's Day, and Chinese people are busy celebrating the New Year, busy enjoying themselves, and living a drunken and dreamlike life, while the Japanese army is practicing bayonet drills in the cold snow, practicing killing, preparing to kill Chinese people! Ah, ah, drunken and dreamlike Chinese people! Still not waking up? The enemy is practicing killing us right in front of us!

My heart was beating, my blood was rushing, I clenched my fists, and I continued to move forward with all my might, walking my path...

Fiction

Scholarly Family (6th Installment) 227

— Wang Zhongxian

"She is much more capable than me!" Zhongnan lit a small cigar with one hand, squinting at Ruohua. "The Great Learning says that those who wish to govern their country must first regulate their family. I am ashamed to say that although I manage the finances of a province, I have no way to manage my own family affairs. You see, since she came to take care of my family, expenses have been saved, and I often have the opportunity to eat local flavors. The upper rooms are also organized, and the people below are also doing things in order. When I spend half a day at home, I don't feel stuffy anymore. Unlike before, when I returned to the mansion, it was like walking into a city of sorrow. If she uses her family management skills to govern the region, I think there will be excellent results!"

"You're making fun of me!" Ruohua glared at Zhongnan with her pretty eyes. The lightning-like gaze instantly shifted from Zhongnan's face to Youzhong's eyes.娇嗔 transformed into娇羞, she smiled charmingly and quickly lowered her head.

"Daddy!" Daiqiu handed a cigar to Zhongnan's mouth with one hand and held a box of洋火 in the other, striking a light for him.

"Good son!" Zhongnan took a puff of smoke and then hugged her in his arms, kissing her apple-like cheeks.

"Fifth Uncle is here. Aren't you going to pay your respects?" Ruohua ordered Daiqiu.

"Fifth Uncle!" Daiqiu bowed respectfully to Youzhong and automatically offered him a cigarette, lighting the洋火 for him in the same way. Youzhong originally smoked, but because it was inconvenient to refuse this young lady's enthusiasm, he had to reluctantly learn to smoke. His smoking posture was not very elegant. Ruohua laughed when she saw it.

"How old are you?" Youzhong also hugged her in his arms, kissing her face.

"Twelve years old," Daiqiu twisted her neck and leaned into Youzhong's arms.

"Fifth Uncle, she can sing! Daiqiu, sing a little lover song for Fifth Uncle. Fifth Uncle will take you to see a movie tomorrow."

Urged by her mother, Daiqiu left Youzhong's arms, singing and making expressions at the same time. She sang very harmoniously and rhythmically. Youzhong clapped his hands and praised her repeatedly. Zhongnan listened with great satisfaction. After watching her finish twisting and turning, he smiled and scolded her, "Little monster!"

While they were laughing happily, a small child with yellow nasal mucus walked in from outside, dragging his feet as he walked up to Zhongnan...

"Daddy! Mom wants you to go."

"What's the matter again?" Zhongnan lowered his face and asked fiercely.

"Mom has a stomachache and wants you to rub her belly."

"Bullshit!" Zhongnan's "shit" word was uttered with twelve points of strength,彈茂生 out of the room. Ruohua looked at Youzhong and laughed. Youzhong burst open his lips, afraid to laugh out loud. Daiqiu hid behind Zhongnan, secretly scraping her grandpa's face.

Zhongnan stood up and apologized, "One child is so cute, and another is so annoying! It shows that a mother's education for children is the most important."
